Slice 139 closed the lookback sweep by wiring 12 schema-only items via the projection pass: Cloak of Protection, Ring of Protection, Stone of Good Luck (each shipping AC + 6 per-ability save modifiers, plus Stone of Good Luck's 6 per-ability check modifiers; the engine's `ModifierTarget` requires discriminated per-ability entries rather than a generic 'save' / 'check' literal, matching the Paladin Aura of Protection precedent), Ring of Warmth, Boots of the Winterlands, and the three Tier-2 condition-immunity / advantage-arm items (Ring of Free Action's paralyzed + restrained immunities, Sentinel Shield's initiative + perception advantage, Gloves of Swimming and Climbing's Athletics advantage). Bracers of Archery still ships schema-only pending a conditional-damage-by-weapon-type primitive (the Archery fighting style's item-sourced analog).
- **Pure narrative / DM-discretion items** (intentionally no engine wiring): Lantern of Revealing (invisible creatures within 30 ft of a lit lantern are visible — engine doesn't track lighting or position), Robe of Useful Items (12 patches plus 4d4 random extras produce DM-resolved objects when torn off).
- **Numeric-bonus templates** (items-batch-1.5): Weapon +1 / +2 / +3 and Armor +1 / +2 / +3. These ship as generic templates rather than specific items (the existing Flametongue Longsword is the only concrete +N weapon). One remaining blocker: for the weapon templates, an extension of the slice-76 `ItemInstance.temporaryBuff` shape (which models *temporary* magical bonuses from spells like Magic Weapon) into a permanent / inherent counterpart, so that a +1 longsword instance carries its attack and damage bonus without a spell effect tagging it. Armor templates now compose cleanly with `AddModifier { target: 'ac', value: N }` via the slice-132 projection. The consumer-side instantiation pattern (overlay template + base weapon / armor) is out of scope for the engine; the pack just ships the template rows so consumers can name them.
- **Items-batch-1.6 RAW-shape blockers** (grouped by primitive):
  - *Positional / spatial anchoring*: Immovable Rod (button-press locks the rod in space, supports up to 8000 lbs). The engine doesn't model positions, so the anchoring itself is consumer-side. Once a position primitive lands, the rod becomes a discoverable "object with infinite mass while activated" annotation; the 8000-lb threshold for breaking the lock fits a simple weight predicate.
  - *Jump-distance derive surface*: Ring of Jumping (cast Jump at will). Same missing primitive as Boots of Striding and Springing's jump-multiplier arm. Composing with the at-will-spell-from-item bullet would let the ring fire the Jump spell with no slot cost.
  - *Object transformation*: Folding Boat (command word converts a 1-foot box into a 10-foot rowboat, second word into a 24-foot sailing ship; third word reverses). Distinct from creature transformations (Wild Shape, Polymorph) since the engine has no inanimate-object schema. Pure consumer-side until a vehicle / object catalog lands.
  - *Vehicle + pilot-controlled actions*: Apparatus of the Crab (large mechanical crab with HP / AC / movement modes, controlled via 10 internal levers each driving a different action). Composes on top of the summon system (slice 48) for the crab as a creature with an inline statblock, plus a pilot-controls primitive the engine doesn't have (the operator inside the crab takes actions that drive the crab's actions). Defer until a pilotable-companion shape is needed for multiple items.
  - *Pure DM-discretion items added this batch* (intentionally no engine wiring): Eversmoking Bottle (releases an obscuring smoke cloud per Fog Cloud's area; the engine doesn't track lighting or obscurement zones), Marvelous Pigments (paints real three-dimensional objects from imagination; pure DM-resolved illusion-of-real-objects), Bag of Beans (3d4 random-effect beans with a 100-entry table per RAW; same shape as Deck of Many Things' deferral, both wait on a random-effects-table primitive), Quaal's Feather Token Anchor (command word anchors a ship; the token vanishes after use). The Feather Token's single-use vanish behavior would compose with the slice-yet-to-land `ConsumeItem` planner from batch 1.3's deferral, treating it as a single-charge magic item rather than a `ConsumableSchema` entry, since RAW catalogs all Feather Tokens as magic items.
- **Items-batch-1.7 charges-bearing wave** (the per-item action wiring; the charges shape itself is now in-pack). Cross-cutting blocker: a `UseItem` planner that walks the activated item's `effects` array, consumes the appropriate charges, and routes the resulting effects (spell-grant casts, damage rolls, condition applications) through the existing planner surface. `UseItem` is the magic-item analog of the `ConsumeItem` planner deferred for batch 1.3's potions: charge-driven instead of single-use, and the item persists after activation. Per-item shapes once `UseItem` lands:
  - *Pearl of Power*: a `RegainSpellSlot { maxLevel: 3 }` effect kind that returns one expended spell slot of level 3 or lower to the wearer's pool. Composes with the existing slot-tracking shape (slots already rebuild per long rest); the new primitive is an item-driven trigger.
  - *Pipes of Haunting*: `ItemSpellGrant` casting Fear (RAW save DC 13 against a 1-minute frightened condition), the same primitive already named for Hat of Disguise and Helm of Telepathy. The charges shape gates each casting at 1 charge per use.
  - *Wind Fan*: `ItemSpellGrant` casting Gust of Wind without the spell's normal concentration requirement (the RAW item version is fire-and-forget). The "20% cumulative chance of tearing into tatters per use" arm needs a brand-new per-use degradation roll primitive; defer that arm and ship the casting once `UseItem` and `ItemSpellGrant` land.
  - *Circlet of Blasting*: `ItemSpellGrant` casting Scorching Ray at a fixed attack bonus of +5 (item caster surrogate). Same blocker as the other spell-grant items; the charges shape limits it to 1/day.
  - *Gem of Brightness*: distinct from the spell-grant pattern. The gem has three actions at different charge costs (0-charge bright light, 1-charge blinding ray with save DC 15, 5-charge cone-of-brilliance blinding all in a 30-ft cone). Needs a multi-action item shape that lets `UseItem` select among per-action effect lists with per-action charge costs, plus an item-disenchant-on-empty state-transition primitive for the "becomes a nonmagical jewel when the last charge is used" RAW arm.
  - *Driftglobe*: composite item with two activation modes. Mode 1 is a continuous bright/dim light radius toggled by command word (needs a `ToggleItemEffect` planner plus a light-radius primitive the engine doesn't track). Mode 2 is `ItemSpellGrant` casting Daylight at 1 charge with dawn recharge. Defer both arms until the underlying primitives land; the charges shape is in place for the Daylight casting.
- **Items-batch-1.8 common-rarity wondrous set** (intentionally pure narrative or DM-discretion; no engine wiring planned for most). The eight commons in this batch fill the previously-empty common tier of the rarity ladder; they ship as schema-only flavor items rather than mechanical primitives in waiting. Per-item shape:
  - *Cloak of Many Fashions* and *Shield of Expression*: cosmetic-only (the cloak changes appearance on command, the shield shifts its emblazoned face). Pure DM-discretion narrative; no primitive needed.
  - *Clothes of Mending*: cosmetic self-repair (clothes mend tears and stains overnight). Pure narrative.
  - *Pole of Angling*: cosmetic fishing tool (turns into a fishing pole with bait and lure on command). Pure narrative.
  - *Hat of Vermin*: a one-charge-equivalent novelty (command word releases 1d4 rats / bats / frogs from the hat once per day). RAW-wise this is closest to a `SummonCreature` planner with a fixed creature table and dawn recharge, but the engine doesn't ship summon-from-item; treat as narrative-only until either summons-from-items or a vermin-table primitive lands. Authored without `charges` because the released creatures themselves aren't a tracked resource at the item layer.
  - *Ear Horn of Hearing*: cures the deafened condition while held (no save, no time limit). Composes with the existing condition vocabulary via a `SuppressCondition { conditionId: 'deafened' }` effect once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack (same blocker as the items-batch-1.1 / 1.2 / 1.4 cohort).
  - *Mystery Key*: unlocks one specific lock the DM chooses when the key is found. Pure narrative (the key's correspondence to a lock is set at game-table time, not at engine layer).
  - *Tankard of Sobriety*: drinking from the tankard renders any liquid non-intoxicating. Pure narrative (the engine doesn't track inebriation).

  Why this batch ships as pure stub even though Ear Horn of Hearing has a clean mechanical wiring path: gating it on a single primitive that's already named for ~6 other items (the magic-item-effect-projection pass plus a `SuppressCondition` shape) means it walks from schema-only to wired in a single coordinated batch with the rest. Authoring it now keeps the common-tier rarity coverage even, and reuses the existing deferral note rather than spawning a new one.
- **Items-batch-1.9 specific named weapons** (extend beyond batch 1.5's generic +N templates with the iconic DMG weapon roster). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'magic'` with `effects: []` and no charges, matching the existing Flametongue Longsword shape rather than the base-weapon shape (consumer-side instantiation overlays the magic-item template onto a base weapon, same as Weapon +1 / +2 / +3). The cross-cutting blocker is still the magic-item-effect-projection pass already named for ~20 wondrous items, plus the permanent-attack-and-damage-bonus extension of the slice-76 `ItemInstance.temporaryBuff` shape that batch 1.5 named. The new per-item shapes this batch introduces:
  - *Vicious Weapon* and *Vorpal Sword*: on-crit special effect. Vicious adds extra 7 damage on a crit; Vorpal severs the target's head on a natural 20 (instant kill on a head-bearing slashing-vulnerable creature). The `planAttack` crit-resolution chain doesn't currently have an item-driven extension point for "additional damage on crit" or "alternate outcome on natural 20"; needs a new `WeaponCritRider { extraDice?, alternateOutcome? }` hook the planner consults when an attack's crit-confirmation arm fires. The Vorpal "head and not immune to slashing" gate is a target-predicate the engine can express today via creature traits.
  - *Sun Blade* and *Holy Avenger*: type-conditional damage rider. Sun Blade adds +2 damage vs Undead and deals radiant damage as its base type; Holy Avenger (paladin-attunement) adds +1d10 radiant vs Fiends and Undead. Composes with the existing damage-rider primitives (`AddModifier { target: 'damage', value: N }` and `AddDamageDice { dice, damageType, when }`) once the conditional-by-target-type-tag fact is available; the engine already tags creatures by type in monster statblocks, so `event.targetType` would be the natural fact addition.
  - *Frost Brand*: composite passive. Extra 1d6 cold damage on hit (same `AddDamageDice` shape Sun Blade and Holy Avenger want); fire resistance while held (same `GrantResistance { damageType: 'fire' }` projection that the magic-item-effect-projection pass enables); extinguishes nonmagical fires within 30 ft (pure narrative). All three arms wire once projection lands except the fire-extinguishing arm which is consumer-side.
  - *Dwarven Thrower*: returns-on-throw + type-conditional damage. The on-throw return is a new shape (the engine has no throw-return primitive); compose-wise it's a "after-throw, item teleports back to wielder's hand" hook on the thrown-weapon attack path. The vs-Giants damage rider shares the type-conditional shape with Holy Avenger / Sun Blade.
  - *Hammer of Thunderbolts*: ability-score-floor enchantment plus a save-or-die on thunder crits. The "STR becomes 27 when wielding the hammer with belt and gauntlets equipped" arm wants an extension of the items-batch-1.2 `OverrideAbilityScore` primitive that gates the override on a multi-item attunement set (predicate: all three items attuned by the wearer). The save-or-die-on-thunder-crit arm composes the new `WeaponCritRider` from Vicious / Vorpal with a CON-save outcome.
  - *Berserker Axe*: item-curse-triggered compulsion plus level-scaled HP boost. The HP-boost ("gain `level` max HP while attuned") wants a `ModifyMaxHP { formula: 'level' }` projection effect — clean wiring once projection lands. The frenzy-curse-on-damage-in-combat arm needs a brand-new item-curse primitive: the engine doesn't model "item the wearer can't voluntarily release" or "compulsion to attack the nearest visible creature on your turn" (the closest neighbor is `ApplyCondition` with charmed / frightened, but compulsion-to-attack-nearest is its own RAW shape). Defer the curse arm; ship the HP-boost in the projection wave.
  - *Attunement-restriction enforcement*: Holy Avenger requires a Paladin; Dwarven Thrower requires a Dwarf. The schema's `attunementCondition: string` field is in place (used by Pearl of Power for "Spellcaster"); the engine's attunement reducer doesn't currently parse this string into a class / species predicate, so the restriction is data-only today. Could wire as a free-text matcher against the bearer's `classId` / `speciesId` once an attunement-precondition gate lands on the attunement planner.
- **Items-batch-1.10 named armors and shields** (the defensive parallel to batch 1.9). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'magic'` with `effects: []` and no charges, matching the existing Cloak of Protection and Armor +1 / +2 / +3 shape (consumer-side overlays the magic-item template onto a base armor or shield, identical pattern to the weapon templates). Cross-cutting blocker remains the magic-item-effect-projection pass plus the slice-76 `ItemInstance.temporaryBuff` extension into a permanent / inherent counterpart that batch 1.5 named for the +N templates. Per-item shapes this batch introduces:
  - *Adamantine Armor*: inbound-attack-crit-rewrite primitive. RAW says any crit against the wearer becomes a normal hit while the armor is worn. The damage-resolution chain doesn't currently expose a "convert crit to normal hit" hook the way armor / item effects could intercept. Composes as `RewriteIncomingCrit` on the wearer's effect stack once projection lands, with the resolver consulting the flag before applying the crit-multiplier branch.
  - *Mithral Armor*: armor-property-suppression. RAW removes both stealth disadvantage and any strength requirement from the underlying medium / heavy armor. Straightforward predicate-modification on the existing `stealthDisadvantage` and `strRequirement` armor fields once projection lands; no new primitive needed.
  - *Elven Chain*: armor-category-override primitive. RAW: counts as light armor for the wearer (so e.g. Stealth checks aren't disadvantaged, DEX cap is removed for AC). Needs a `ReclassifyArmor { newCategory: 'light' }` effect that overrides the base armor's category in the AC and proficiency-check derivations. New primitive, single user.
  - *Glamoured Studded Leather*: bonus-action appearance change. Pure narrative (the wearer chooses an appearance the armor can mimic). Composes with a future `UseItem` planner for the activation step, but the cosmetic-change result is consumer-side; defer entirely to narrative.
  - *Dragon Scale Mail*: resistance-by-dragon-color plus the +1 AC bonus the entry also carries. The AC bonus composes with `AddModifier { target: 'ac', value: 1 }` once projection lands. The resistance arm wants `GrantResistance { damageType }` where the damage type is chosen at item-instantiation time per the dragon color the scales came from (acid for black, lightning for blue, cold for white, fire for red, etc.); needs an item-instance "variant" field the engine doesn't currently model, or a per-instance configuration that the consumer fills in. Defer the variant arm; the AC bonus wires for free.
  - *Demon Armor*: item-curse plus offensive-claw grant. The cursed-and-can't-doff-voluntarily arm composes with the Berserker Axe item-curse primitive from batch 1.9. The "fiendish claws" arm is novel: the armor grants the wearer a natural-weapon attack (claws dealing 1d8 + STR slashing). Needs a `GrantNaturalAttack { name, dice, damageType, ability }` effect kind the engine doesn't model (closest is a planner that creates a virtual weapon instance and adds it to the wearer's available attack list). Single user today but generalizes to monk unarmed strikes, drake breath weapons, and tabaxi claws across content yet to ship.
  - *Sentinel Shield*: ✓ wired in slice 139. Both arms ship as `SetAdvantage` entries (`on: 'initiative'` + `on: { kind: 'skill', skill: 'perception' }`). No deferred sub-arms.
  - *Spellguard Shield*: composite save-and-attack defense. Advantage on saving throws against spells (composes with `SetAdvantage { on: 'save', savedAgainst: 'spell' }`; needs a "save against spell" predicate the existing save shape doesn't carry). Plus: spell attacks against the wearer have disadvantage (needs an inbound-attack-disadvantage primitive scoped to spell attacks specifically, related to but distinct from the conditional-disadvantage shape Cloak of Elvenkind wants). Two new sub-predicates; same projection blocker as the rest.
- **Items-batch-1.11 rod / staff / wand cohort** (the charges shape is in-pack; per-item action wiring routes through the same `UseItem` planner deferred for batch 1.7). All eight items in this batch are charges-bearing per RAW. Cross-cutting blocker is the `UseItem` planner from batch 1.7's deferral: walks the activated item's effect array, consumes the appropriate charges, and routes resulting effects (spell-grant casts, damage rolls, condition applications) through the existing planner surface. Per-item shapes once `UseItem` lands:
  - *Rod of the Pact Keeper +1*: composite passive plus active. The passive arm (+1 to warlock spell attack rolls and DC) wires once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack (the magic-item-effect-projection pass already named for ~20 wondrous items) plus a "warlock spell scope" predicate the engine doesn't currently carry. The active arm (regain one expended warlock spell slot, 1/day) is the same `RegainSpellSlot` primitive Pearl of Power named in batch 1.7, with the additional constraint that the slot must come from the warlock class's slot pool specifically (multiclassed warlocks need the engine to disambiguate). The +2 / +3 variants compose with the same primitives at higher numeric values.
  - *Staff of the Adder*: bonus-action transformation into a giant constrictor snake. Same `SummonCreature` shape Hat of Vermin's batch-1.8 entry waited on, but with a fixed creature ID (giant constrictor snake from the monsters lane) and an item-bound lifecycle (the snake reverts to staff form when it takes damage). Once `UseItem` and `SummonCreature` land, the staff wires as a 1-charge-per-dawn invocation of the summon. The "reverts on damage" arm wants a damage-triggered despawn hook on the summon, which would generalize to other transformation items.
  - *Staff of Charming*: at-will spell casting via charges. Casts Charm Person at 1 charge (or save DC override 17 for the staff). Same `ItemSpellGrant` primitive Hat of Disguise and Helm of Telepathy named in batch 1.2, plus a per-cast save-DC-override hook the existing spell vocabulary doesn't carry (the spell's DC comes from the caster, not the item; the staff dictates DC 17 regardless of wielder). Two RAW spell modes (Charm Person and Command), each at 1 charge. Plus an absorption sub-shape: when targeted by a charm or command, the staff can absorb the incoming spell as a reaction and recover a charge equal to the absorbed spell's level. Absorption is its own primitive, distinct from the magic-missile-immunity sub-shape Brooch of Shielding wanted.
  - *Staff of Healing*: at-will Cure Wounds / Lesser Restoration / Mass Cure Wounds via charges (1 / 2 / 5 charges respectively). Same `ItemSpellGrant` primitive Staff of Charming wants, with the level-spend lookup choosing which spell the wielder is casting. The healing-output values use the staff's progression (e.g. Cure Wounds at 2d8+2 regardless of wielder spell level) rather than the wielder's slot level; needs an item-level-progression override that's distinct from the wielder's spell-slot choice.
  - *Wand of Web*: 1-charge-per-cast Web spell at save DC 15. Pure `ItemSpellGrant` once it lands with the staff-style fixed save DC.
  - *Wand of Magic Detection*: 1-charge-per-cast Detect Magic spell. Same shape as Wand of Web; this one is the first charges-bearing wand in the pack without attunement.
  - *Wand of Fireballs*: variable-charge spell scaling. 1 charge casts Fireball at 3rd level, with 1 additional charge per level above that (up to 7th-level Fireball if all charges are spent). Same `ItemSpellGrant` primitive plus a variable-charges-per-cast extension the simpler wands don't need (Wand of Magic Missiles ships with the simpler "1 charge per cast plus 1 per slot level above 1st" but the engine doesn't yet enforce this either).
  - *Wand of Wonder*: random-effect-table primitive. RAW: roll d100 on a 90+ entry table to determine what happens (each entry naming a spell, area effect, or narrative outcome). Same shape as Bag of Beans and Deck of Many Things deferred in earlier batches; all three wait on a `RollOnRandomTable { tableId }` primitive plus a content-pack table-of-effects shape that the magic-item schema doesn't currently model. The "table-of-effects" shape generalizes to wild-magic surges and other random-result mechanics across content yet to ship.
- **Items-batch-1.12 potions and oils** (route through the `ConsumeItem` planner deferred for batch 1.3's potion set; all eight ship as `onConsume: []` with narrative descriptions). Cross-cutting blocker is unchanged from batch 1.3: a `ConsumeItem` planner walks the consumable's `onConsume` array on activation, fires each Effect against the consumer, and emits the appropriate events. Per-potion variant shapes the planner would compose:
  - *Potion of Water Breathing*: `ApplyCondition` with a 1-hour duration carrying the breathlessness marker effect Necklace of Adaptation's batch-1.2 deferral named. Once both `ConsumeItem` and the breathlessness marker land, this potion wires as a single composition.
  - *Potion of Fire Breath*: composite consume-then-charges. The drink installs a 3-charge / 1-hour-duration condition on the consumer; each charge spend triggers a bonus-action breath-weapon attack (4d6 fire damage, DC 13 DEX save for half, 30-ft single-target range). Needs the `ConsumeItem` planner plus a "condition-with-internal-charges" extension of the existing condition shape (no precedent in the wired catalog — most conditions count down rounds or minutes, not uses). Plus a breath-weapon attack primitive scoped to a single target (the engine has cone / line / sphere area shapes from `AreaEffectSpell` but not "ranged single-target attack rooted in the user's mouth").
  - *Potion of Hill Giant Strength*: 1-hour `OverrideAbilityScore { ability: 'STR', value: 21 }` condition (the primitive batch 1.2 named for the Belt of Hill Giant Strength). Once both `ConsumeItem` and `OverrideAbilityScore` land, the potion and the belt share the same wiring at the same numeric value. The remaining giant-strength tier (Stone 23 / Frost 23 / Fire 25 / Cloud 27 / Storm 29) ships in a future batch under the same primitive at different `value` targets.
  - *Oil of Slipperiness*: dual-target consumable. Applied to a creature, grants the effect of the Freedom of Movement spell as a `ApplyCondition` with 8-hour duration carrying the spell's effect set (Freedom of Movement is currently schema-only). Applied to a surface, creates a difficult-terrain zone with a DC 10 DEX-save-vs-prone trigger for any creature entering it. Needs `ConsumeItem` plus a target-selection branch (the consume planner consults a `consumeChoice` field to pick which arm fires) plus the Freedom of Movement spell wiring plus a difficult-terrain-zone primitive that doesn't exist yet (the engine has area-effect spells but no persistent passive difficult-terrain markers on a tile or square).
  - *Potion of Invisibility*: `ApplyCondition` with the existing Invisible condition for 1 hour, with the "ends on attack or cast a spell" trigger from the Invisibility spell. Once `ConsumeItem` lands, this wires by composition: the Invisible condition vocabulary is in-pack, and the spell-ends-on-attack hook exists in the existing Invisibility spell wiring.
  - *Potion of Flying*: 1-hour `ApplyCondition` carrying `ModifySpeed { mode: 'fly', op: 'set' }` at a value equal to the consumer's walking speed at consume time. The `ModifySpeed { mode: 'fly' }` primitive is shipped (slice 77); the "value equal to walking speed at consume time" arm needs the consume planner to read the consumer's walking-speed derivation and bake it into the condition's effect at consume time. Plus the "falls if still aloft when the duration ends" arm is consumer-side / DM-discretion.
  - *Potion of Speed*: `ApplyCondition` for 1 minute carrying the Haste spell's effect set (additional action, +2 AC, advantage on DEX saves, doubled speed) without the concentration requirement. Haste is currently schema-only at L3 in the spell catalog; once it wires plus `ConsumeItem` lands, the potion composes with a single deviation (the concentration arm is suppressed for the potion variant). Plus the post-effect "lethargic for 1 minute, can't move or take actions" arm needs the engine to chain a follow-up condition onto a condition's expiry (no precedent in the wired catalog).
  - *Oil of Sharpness*: weapon-targeted consumable rather than creature-targeted. Applied to a piercing or slashing weapon (or up to 5 pieces of ammunition), grants +3 to attack and damage rolls and counts as magical for 1 hour. Needs `ConsumeItem` to route into the weapon-instance buff shape (slice 76's `ItemInstance.temporaryBuff` already models a temporary attack-and-damage bonus applied via a spell-tag; the oil's application path is the new wiring). Stacks with the batch-1.5 weapon templates exactly as the +N templates would expect.
- **Items-batch-1.13 spell scrolls** (fills the previously-empty scroll category; eight reference entries spanning cantrip through 9th level across all five non-artifact rarities). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'consumable'` with `onConsume: []` and a narrative description that names the underlying spell, the scroll-fixed save DC / spell attack bonus, and the non-class-list read-check DC per RAW. The scroll category is currently a sub-pattern of `consumable` rather than a distinct `itemKind: 'scroll'` discriminator (the schema would need extension to model scrolls as a first-class category with explicit `spellId`, `castLevel`, `saveDC`, `attackBonus`, and `readCheckDC` fields). Wiring per arm:
  - *Cross-cutting blocker* (same as the batch-1.3 and batch-1.12 potions): a `ConsumeItem` planner walks the consumable's `onConsume` array and routes resulting effects. Scrolls compose the planner with a fixed-DC `ItemSpellGrant` (the staff-of-charming variant batch 1.11 named, where the spell's save DC and attack bonus come from the item rather than the wielder). Single-use semantics: the planner deletes or marks-spent the consumable instance after a successful cast.
  - *Class-list gating arm*: RAW says scrolls on the consumer's class list cast as a normal spell; off-list casters must succeed on a DC `10 + spellLevel` INT or WIS check (consumer choice) to cast at all. Failure destroys the scroll without effect for level-1+ scrolls; cantrip scrolls just don't fire. Needs an "is this spell on the consumer's class list" predicate the engine doesn't currently expose (the class schemas carry per-class spell lists, but no derive helper unifies them into a "consumer can natively cast `spellId`" query) plus an ability-check resolution path the consume planner can branch on.
  - *Per-level scaling*: scroll save DC and attack bonus scale with spell level (DC 13 / +5 for L0–L2, DC 15 / +7 for L3–L4, DC 17 / +9 for L5–L6, DC 18 / +10 for L7–L8, DC 19 / +11 for L9). The eight entries in this batch ship the scroll-side numbers in the description; once the schema gains explicit `saveDC` and `attackBonus` fields on scroll-shaped consumables, the values move into structured data and the planner consumes them directly.
  - *Concentration handling* (Greater Invisibility, plus any concentration spell wired through scrolls): the consumer becomes the spell's concentration anchor for the scroll-cast spell's duration. This composes cleanly with the existing concentration-tracker once `ConsumeItem` + `ItemSpellGrant` land; no new primitive needed beyond what scrolls share with potion-of-speed-style "Haste without concentration" (here, concentration is preserved rather than suppressed).
  - *Risk-clause spells* (Wish, and arguably Disintegrate for the dust-on-kill clause): the spell itself carries its post-cast complications (Wish's 33% stress arm, the never-cast-Wish-again risk on certain Wish variants). Once Wish wires, the scroll inherits the entire complication chain because it routes through the existing spell wiring rather than reproducing it.
- **Items-batch-1.14 Ioun Stones** (introduces the Ioun Stone family with one passive stone per ability score plus Awareness and Protection). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'magic'` with `effects: []`, all very rare or rare, all attunement-required. The Ioun Stone orbiting mechanic (the stone hovers around the wearer's head and doesn't occupy a body slot) is currently model-implicit: the engine treats Ioun Stones as attuned items with no equipped slot, which already works for the magic-item shape since the slot system is consumer-side metadata. RAW only enforces the orbiting visual narratively; defer that to consumer rendering. Per-stone shapes once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack:
  - *Ability-score Ioun Stones* (Strength, Agility, Fortitude, Intellect, Insight, Leadership): each increases the named ability score by 2, to a maximum of 20. Mechanically distinct from batch 1.2's Belt of Hill Giant Strength (`OverrideAbilityScore { value: 21 }` which sets the score) and batch 1.9's Hammer of Thunderbolts (multi-item attunement setting STR to 27). The Ioun Stones want an `IncreaseAbilityScore { ability: AbilityScore, amount: 2, cap: 20 }` primitive that stacks additively up to a cap, distinct from the set / override semantic. Two different primitives serve the family: `OverrideAbilityScore` for set-to-N items (belt, headband, gauntlets), `IncreaseAbilityScore` for additive-with-cap items (Ioun Stones, Tome of Clear Thought / Quickness / Leadership family that ships in a future batch under the same primitive at `amount: 2, cap: 20` then permanently bumps the user's base score on consumption).
  - *Ioun Stone (Awareness)*: surprise-immunity. RAW: "You can't be surprised while you're conscious." Composes with a `GrantConditionImmunity` shape pointed at the engine's surprise mechanic; in 2024 surprise is a disadvantage on initiative rather than a tracked condition, so the cleanest wiring is a `SuppressInitiativeDisadvantage { source: 'surprise' }` or equivalent predicate that's distinct from the conditional-disadvantage primitive Cloak of Elvenkind / Eyes of the Eagle want (those are checks against the wearer; this is the wearer's own initiative roll).
  - *Ioun Stone (Protection)*: ✓ wired in slice 139 as `AddModifier { target: 'ac', value: 1 }`. No deferred sub-arms.
  - *Deferred Ioun Stones*: the charges-style variants (Absorption stores 20 spell levels, Greater Absorption stores 50, Reserve stores 3 levels of spells) ship in a future charges-bearing batch under a "spell-level-pool" charges shape that's distinct from the integer-charges shape Wand of Magic Missiles uses. The legendary variants (Mastery for +1 proficiency bonus, Regeneration for 15 HP per hour, Greater Absorption) ship in a future batch under primitives the engine doesn't currently model: proficiency-bonus override and out-of-combat regeneration with hourly tick semantics.
- **Items-batch-1.15 rings cohort** (extends the existing Ring of Protection / Swimming / Jumping set with eight more entries spanning uncommon through legendary). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'magic'` with `effects: []` and no charges (the charges-bearing rings — Evasion, Shooting Stars, Spell Storing, Spell Turning, Telekinesis, the Ram, Three Wishes, X-Ray Vision, Animal Influence — defer to a future charges-bearing batch under the existing `UseItem` planner blocker from batch 1.7). Per-ring wiring once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack:
  - *Ring of Feather Falling*: trigger-on-fall mechanic. RAW: "When you fall while wearing this ring, you descend 60 feet per round and take no damage from falling." Needs a fall-event hook the engine doesn't currently expose (falling is consumer-narrative today; the engine has no falling planner or fall-damage derivation) plus an auto-cast of Feather Fall's mechanical effect (no concentration, single-target self). Once a falling primitive lands, the ring composes with Feather Fall's existing spell wiring on the trigger.
  - *Ring of Mind Shielding*: composite detection-immunity. RAW: "You are immune to magic that allows other creatures to read your thoughts, determine whether you are lying, know your alignment, or know your creature type. Creatures can telepathically communicate with you only if you allow it. You can use an action to cause the ring to become invisible." Needs a "telepathic detection" predicate plus Detect Thoughts / Zone of Truth / Detect Alignment-style spell immunity (a spell-list-scoped immunity that's distinct from a single-spell immunity like Brooch of Shielding's magic-missile immunity). The "can become invisible" cosmetic arm is narrative.
  - *Ring of Warmth*: ✓ cold-resistance arm wired in slice 139 as `GrantResistance { damageType: 'cold' }`. The temperature-tolerance-to-zero-F arm stays consumer / DM-discretion narrative (the engine doesn't track ambient temperature).
  - *Ring of Water Walking*: walk-on-liquid-surface mechanic. RAW: "While wearing this ring, you can stand on and move across any liquid surface as if it were solid ground." The engine doesn't currently model walking-on-water as a movement primitive (it's a special movement mode distinct from walk / fly / climb / swim). Needs either a `ModifySpeed { mode: 'water-walk', op: 'add' }` extension to the existing `ModifySpeed` primitive that already handles climb / swim / fly, or a composition with the existing Water Walking spell's continuous effect.
  - *Ring of Free Action*: ✓ paralyzed + restrained immunity arms wired in slice 139 as two `GrantConditionImmunity` entries. The difficult-terrain-movement-cost-suppression arm (a per-bearer predicate distinct from slice 90's terrain-layer doubling) and the magical-speed-reduction-immunity arm (needs a magical-vs-nonmagical distinction on speed reductions the engine doesn't currently model) stay deferred.
  - *Ring of Resistance*: variant-typed resistance. RAW: "You have resistance to one damage type while wearing this ring. The damage type is determined by the ring's gem (sapphire = lightning, jade = poison, pearl = acid, ruby = fire, topaz = cold, etc.)." Same item-instance variant pattern as batch 1.10's Dragon Scale Mail (consumer picks damage type at attunement / pack-load time); composes with `GrantResistance { damageType }` once projection lands. The variant arm is shared with Dragon Scale Mail's deferral.
  - *Ring of Regeneration*: out-of-combat HP regeneration with a 10-minute tick. RAW: "While wearing this ring, you regain 1d6 hit points every 10 minutes, provided that you have at least 1 hit point. If you lose a body part, the ring causes the missing part to regrow and return to full functionality after 1d6+1 days." Same shape as the Ioun Stone Regeneration variant deferred in batch 1.14, but at a 10-minute tick rather than hourly. Needs a continuous-HP-regen primitive scoped to a time interval the engine doesn't currently model (rest mechanics handle long-rest / short-rest healing, but not an in-game 10-minute timer for continuous regen). The limb-regrowth arm is consumer-narrative.
  - *Ring of Invisibility*: toggleable Invisible condition. RAW: "While wearing this ring, you can turn invisible as an action. Anything you are wearing or carrying is invisible with you. You remain invisible until the ring is removed, until you attack or cast a spell, or until you use a bonus action to become visible again." Same Invisible-condition primitive as Potion of Invisibility (already in-pack via the wired Invisibility spell), but toggleable rather than 1-hour timed. Needs a `ToggleItemEffect` planner (the same primitive Driftglobe's continuous-light arm deferred in batch 1.7) plus the "ends on attack or spell" trigger that the Invisibility spell already carries. Once both `ToggleItemEffect` and the spell wiring compose, the ring wires cleanly.
- **Items-batch-1.16 Giant Strength tier extension** (completes the canonical Belt + Potion family that batches 1.2 and 1.12 began with Hill Giant Strength). Five belts (`itemKind: 'magic'`, attunement-required, `effects: []`) and five potions (`itemKind: 'consumable'`, `onConsume: []`) covering the Stone (STR 23), Frost (STR 23), Fire (STR 25), Cloud (STR 27), and Storm (STR 29) tiers. All ten ship as pure stub; snapshot-clean. Mechanically the entire family wires through a single primitive — the `OverrideAbilityScore { ability: 'STR', value: N }` shape that batch 1.2's Belt of Hill Giant Strength named — at six different `value` targets (21 / 23 / 23 / 25 / 27 / 29). The Frost and Stone tiers ship at the same numeric target (STR 23); they're distinct items per RAW because their visual / flavor differs and their crafting components differ, but their mechanical wiring is identical. Belt rarities follow the RAW progression (Hill rare, Stone / Frost / Fire very rare, Cloud / Storm legendary); potion rarities are one tier lower across the board per RAW (Hill uncommon, Stone / Frost / Fire rare, Cloud very rare, Storm legendary), reflecting the 1-hour duration limit on the potion variant. The cross-cutting projection blocker is unchanged from batch 1.2; the consume-side `ConsumeItem` blocker is unchanged from batch 1.3. No new primitives this batch.
- **Items-batch-1.17 robes and outer garments** (the canonical 5e/2024 DMG robe catalog is short — only four robes total, two of which are charges-bearing and deferred — so this batch extends to thematically-adjacent outer-garment slot items: two robes, two cloaks, bracers, two pairs of boots, plus a cosmetic-common armor entry). Per-item shapes once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack:
  - *Robe of the Archmagi*: composite caster-bonus passive. +2 AC, +2 spell save DC, +2 spell attack bonus, advantage on saving throws against spells. The +2 AC arm composes with `AddModifier { target: 'ac', value: 2 }` (the shape Ring of Protection and Cloak of Protection use). The save / attack +2 arms compose with the same `AddModifier` shape targeted at the bearer's spell-save-DC and spell-attack derivations once projection lands. The advantage-on-saves-vs-spells arm composes with `SetAdvantage { on: 'save', savedAgainst: 'spell' }` (the predicate Spellguard Shield wanted in batch 1.10). The class-locked attunement is data-only today (same shape as Holy Avenger from batch 1.9).
  - *Robe of Eyes*: composite passive-sense bundle. 360-degree vision (no flanking-from-behind once flanking is modeled), darkvision 120 ft, see invisible, see ethereal, advantage on Perception checks involving sight, can't be surprised, cannot be blinded by sighted-source effects except by sunlight. Composes with `GrantSense` (slice 127) at multiple sense entries (`darkvision`, `seeInvisible`, `seeEthereal`), `SuppressInitiativeDisadvantage { source: 'surprise' }` from Ioun Stone (Awareness) in batch 1.14, and conditional perception advantage from Sentinel Shield in batch 1.10. The sunlight-blinded sub-arm needs an action-tagged-as-looking trigger that fires the Blinded condition when the wearer takes a Search-like action while looking at a sunlight source.
  - *Cloak of Displacement*: bearer-protective disadvantage on incoming attacks. Same third-party-perspective conditional-disadvantage shape as Cloak of Elvenkind (batch 1.1, perception-scoped) and Spellguard Shield (batch 1.10, spell-attack-scoped), but here scoped to all incoming weapon attacks. Plus the "ceases to function until your next turn after you take damage" arm needs a damage-event-triggered suspension on the projected effect (a new "effect goes dormant for N rounds on trigger event T" primitive that generalizes to several other RAW items in the long tail).
  - *Cloak of Billowing*: cosmetic dramatic billow. Pure narrative; no engine wiring needed.
  - *Bracers of Defense*: conditional +2 AC. RAW: "+2 bonus to AC if you are wearing no armor and using no shield." Composes with the same `AddModifier { target: 'ac', value: 2 }` shape Ring of Protection uses, gated by a predicate on the bearer's equipment state (`bearer.armorEquipped == null && bearer.shieldEquipped == null`). The predicate is consumer-side metadata until the engine's equipped-item shape gains explicit slot accessors.
  - *Boots of Levitation*: at-will Levitate spell. Same `ItemSpellGrant { spellId: 'levitate', atWill: true }` primitive Hat of Disguise wanted in batch 1.2.
  - *Boots of Speed*: toggleable speed-doubling with per-day time budget plus opportunity-attack disadvantage. Composes with `ModifySpeed { mode: 'walk', op: 'multiply', factor: 2 }` (the multiply op was named for `Boots of Striding and Springing` batch-1.2 deferral); the OAs-against-you disadvantage is the same third-party-perspective shape Cloak of Displacement wants but scoped to opportunity attacks specifically; the per-day 10-minute time budget is the same `timeBudget` shape Winged Boots wanted in batch 1.4, plus a `ToggleItemEffect` planner the Driftglobe / Ring of Invisibility deferred.
  - *Smoldering Armor*: cosmetic smoke wisps when the wearer takes damage. Pure narrative; no engine wiring needed.
- **Items-batch-1.18 cloaks and small-slot accessories** (widened framing because the canonical 5e/2024 cloak slot is thin once batch 1.17 absorbed Displacement and Billowing — only Cloak of the Manta Ray remains as pure stub, Cloak of Arachnida and Cape of the Mountebank are both charges-bearing and deferred). The batch pulls the natural slot-adjacent cohort (neck-slot amulets / periapts / talismans, face / head / hands / feet small accessories) so the cloak shipment doesn't ship as a singleton. Per-item shapes once magic-item passive effects project to the wearer's stack:
  - *Cloak of the Manta Ray*: ✓ swim-speed arm wired in slice 139 as `ModifySpeed { mode: 'swim', op: 'set', value: 60 }`. The breathe-underwater arm still needs the breathlessness-marker shape Necklace of Adaptation deferred (batch 1.2); stays deferred.
  - *Amulet of Proof Against Detection and Location*: composite divination-immunity. RAW: "You are hidden from divination magic. You can't be targeted by such magic or perceived through magical scrying sensors." Same spell-list-scoped immunity predicate Ring of Mind Shielding wanted in batch 1.15, but scoped to the divination school rather than telepathic spells specifically (the engine has spells tagged with school in its catalog, so the predicate `event.spell.school === 'divination'` is the natural extension once spell-school is exposed as a fact).
  - *Periapt of Health*: disease immunity plus disease suppression while worn. RAW: "Immune to contracting any disease while you wear this pendant. If already infected, the effects are suppressed while worn." The disease shape isn't currently modeled at the engine layer (no `Disease` condition or status tracker; it's narrative); `SuppressCondition { conditionId: 'diseased' }` could wire once a disease-marker is added to the conditions vocabulary, but the entire disease pipeline is consumer-side until then.
  - *Talisman of the Sphere*: composite proficiency-doubling-on-specific-checks plus Sphere-of-Annihilation control. RAW: "Double your proficiency bonus on any ability check made to control a Sphere of Annihilation while attuned." The doubling shape composes with an existing `AddModifier { target: 'check' }` if the existing check-bonus shape accepts a "multiplier-by-proficiency" variant; otherwise needs a new `DoubleProficiencyOn { check: predicate }` primitive (the Bard's Jack of All Trades and Rogue's Expertise both use a similar shape internally, so the primitive exists in the engine; this just exposes it for items). The Sphere-of-Annihilation grasp-and-control arm is consumer-narrative (the engine doesn't model the sphere as a tracked object today).
  - *Eyes of Minute Seeing*: conditional advantage on close-range Investigation checks. RAW: "Advantage on Intelligence (Investigation) checks that rely on sight while searching an area or studying an object within 1 foot." Composes with the conditional-advantage shape on Investigation (the Sentinel Shield's wears-side advantage primitive from batch 1.10, scoped to a different skill and gated by a range predicate the engine doesn't currently expose since position isn't modeled). The 1-foot range arm is consumer-narrative until position is modeled.
  - *Helm of Comprehending Languages*: at-will Comprehend Languages plus Insight advantage on spoken-word checks. RAW: "Advantage on Wisdom (Insight) checks made to understand the spoken word of a humanoid. You can also use an action to cast Comprehend Languages from the helm at will." The at-will spell arm composes with `ItemSpellGrant { spellId: 'comprehend-languages', atWill: true }` (the Hat of Disguise / Boots of Levitation primitive). The conditional advantage arm composes with `SetAdvantage { on: 'check', skill: 'insight' }` gated by a spoken-word predicate.
  - *Gloves of Thievery*: +5 to specific Dexterity checks. RAW: "+5 bonus to Dexterity (Sleight of Hand) checks and Dexterity checks made to pick locks." Composes with `AddModifier { target: 'check', value: 5 }` gated by a per-check-kind predicate (Sleight of Hand and lockpicking specifically, not all DEX checks). The lockpicking arm is currently consumer-side (the engine doesn't separate lockpicking from other DEX checks); the Sleight of Hand arm wires straightforwardly via the skill predicate.
  - *Boots of the Winterlands*: ✓ cold-resistance arm wired in slice 139 as `GrantResistance { damageType: 'cold' }`. The ice-and-snow difficult-terrain-ignore arm (needs `IgnoreDifficultTerrain { source: 'ice-or-snow' }` per-bearer predicate, distinct from slice 90's terrain-layer doubling) and the temperature-tolerance arm (consumer-narrative as in Ring of Warmth) stay deferred.
- **Items-batch-1.19 charges-bearing rings** (the followup to the batch-1.15 pure-stub rings cohort, completing the rings catalog with the charges-bearing variants). All eight ship as `itemKind: 'magic'` with the canonical RAW charges shape (5 / never for Spell Storing's spell-level pool, 3 / never for Three Wishes as a single-use-pool ring matching Gem of Brightness's exhaust-then-mundane shape, 1 / longRest for X-Ray Vision, 3 + 1d3 / dawn for Ram / Evasion / Animal Influence / Spell Turning, 6 / dawn for Shooting Stars). Snapshot refresh required (the diff is exactly eight new IDs added to `withChargesIds`); the per-ring action wiring routes through the same `UseItem` planner already deferred for batches 1.7 and 1.11. Per-ring shapes once `UseItem` lands:
  - *Ring of Spell Storing*: stores up to 5 levels of spell into the ring, casts stored spells out as actions. Schema models the level count as charges (max: 5, recharge: never), but the actual mechanic is a spell-level pool: when a spellcaster casts a spell into the ring, the ring stores it and consumes the spell's level from its remaining capacity; when the wearer casts out, the stored spell fires using the ring's stored DC and the level it was stored at. The "refills via inbound cast" arm is a novel shape — distinct from both `RegainSpellSlot` (Pearl of Power) and standard charges. Needs a `CastSpellIntoItem` planner that consumes the caster's spell slot, validates the level fits in the remaining pool, and stores the spell-id + cast-level + DC tuple inside the item-instance.
  - *Ring of Three Wishes*: 3 charges of Wish on a single-use pool that never refills. RAW: "becomes a nonmagical band when the last charge is used." Same exhaust-then-mundane shape as Gem of Brightness from batch 1.7; needs the same item-disenchant-on-empty primitive (`OnExhaust { result: 'remove-magic' }`). Per-charge effect is `ItemSpellGrant { spellId: 'wish' }` once that primitive lands.
  - *Ring of X-Ray Vision*: 1 use per long rest of see-through-walls. The vision-grant arm composes with `GrantSense { sense: 'x-ray', range: 30 }` (slice 127's shape extended to a new sense kind) on a 1-minute duration condition. The post-effect "DC 15 CON save or 1 level of exhaustion" arm composes with the post-effect chained-follow-up-condition primitive Potion of Speed's batch-1.12 deferral named.
  - *Ring of the Ram*: variable-charge attack with three usage tiers. Spend 1-3 charges as an action for a ranged push attack (1 charge = 1d10 force + 5 ft push, 2 charges = 2d10 + 10 ft, 3 charges = 3d10 + 15 ft). Needs the variable-charges-per-cast extension Wand of Fireballs deferred in batch 1.11 plus a directional-push primitive distinct from the `Shove` action (this is a ranged push, not a melee one).
  - *Ring of Evasion*: 1-charge reaction to succeed on a failed DEX save. Composes with `RewriteSaveResult { from: 'fail', to: 'success' }` on the wearer's reaction-window, the same shape as Cloak of Protection's "+1 to all saves" but operating on the outcome rather than the modifier (and gated to DEX saves specifically per RAW). New primitive.
  - *Ring of Animal Influence*: variable-cost spell-grant. 1 charge for Animal Friendship, 1 for Speak with Animals, 2 for Fear (limited to beasts only). Composes with `ItemSpellGrant` at per-spell save-DC override (DC 13 per RAW for the ring), plus the variable-charge cost extension Wand of Fireballs / Ring of the Ram want.
  - *Ring of Shooting Stars*: multi-effect charge pool with dusk-only activation. Three sub-effects each with their own charge cost (Faerie Fire 1, Ball Lightning 1-4, Shooting Stars 2). Needs the multi-action item shape Gem of Brightness deferred in batch 1.7 plus a time-of-day predicate (dusk-only activation) that's distinct from the existing day / night fact (`when: 'dusk-or-darker'`).
  - *Ring of Spell Turning*: reaction to redirect or absorb a targeted spell. Spend 1-3 charges to redirect a spell back at the caster (DC 17 caster-save or be hit by their own spell, per 2014 RAW). Composes with the spell-reflection shape (a new primitive — no existing item or feature in the engine reflects spells back at the caster) plus the variable-charge cost extension.
- **Items-batch-1.20 charges-bearing wand expansion** (extends the batch-1.11 wand cohort with eight more entries, primarily save-or-suffer spell-grant wands). All eight share the canonical 7-charges / 1d6+1-at-dawn shape (Fear / Lightning Bolts / Paralysis / Polymorph / Binding / Pyrotechnics) or the 3-charges / 1d3-at-dawn shape (Enemy Detection / Secrets), matching the existing Wand of Magic Missiles and Wand of Fireballs precedents. Most route through the same `ItemSpellGrant` primitive Staff of Charming and the batch-1.11 wands need. Per-wand shapes once `UseItem` lands:
  - *Wand of Fear*, *Wand of Lightning Bolts*, *Wand of Paralysis*, *Wand of Polymorph*, *Wand of Binding*: variants of the same shape Wand of Fireballs / Wand of Web wanted in batch 1.11 — `ItemSpellGrant { spellId, saveDC: 15 }` (or DC 17 for Polymorph per RAW) with charge consumption gated by the cast. Polymorph specifically also wants the target-creature-form variant that the Polymorph spell wiring carries; the wand inherits that complication chain via the spell wiring. No new primitives beyond the batch-1.11 set; this batch deepens the wand catalog rather than introducing novel shapes.
  - *Wand of Enemy Detection*: 1-charge action grants a 1-minute "sense of enemies within 60 ft" effect. Composes with `GrantSense { sense: 'enemy-detection', range: 60 }` (slice-127 shape extended to a new sense kind; same pattern as Ring of X-Ray Vision's batch-1.19 deferral). Plus a "creatures hostile to the wielder" predicate distinct from the alignment-detect shape Amulet of Proof Against Detection wants — this one is intent-based ("hostile to you specifically"), not alignment-based.
  - *Wand of Secrets*: 1-charge action reveals a hidden door or trap within 30 ft. Composes with a "detect-hidden-object" primitive scoped to the wielder's narrative-discoverable secrets within a range. The engine doesn't currently track hidden-door / hidden-trap state at the entity layer (these are typically narrated by the DM during exploration); pure consumer-side narrative until a discoverable-object schema lands.
  - *Wand of Pyrotechnics*: 1-charge action creates a fireworks display or smoke cloud. Two sub-effects branching on the wielder's choice at activation (pyrotechnics vs smoke cloud). Pyrotechnics: 1d4 fire damage to creatures within 5 ft and blinded condition (DC 13 CON save) for the round. Smoke cloud: 20-ft sphere of obscured terrain for 1 minute. Composes with `ItemSpellGrant` routed to a sub-spell catalog (a wand-internal effect list rather than a published spell), plus a target-selection-at-activation arm distinct from the bearer-vs-surface branch Oil of Slipperiness wanted in batch 1.12 (this one selects between two distinct effect sets).

## Monsters

Two hundred fourteen statblocks.

**Plant + Giant + Misc closure, content-monsters-batch-5.6 (6):** Shrieker Fungus (CR 0), Violet Fungus (CR 1/4), Rust Monster (CR 1/2), Ettin (CR 4), Troll (CR 5), Oni (CR 7). Closes the SRD 5.2.1 Plant catalog (4 to 6 entries — the canonical Awakened Shrub / Awakened Tree / Shambling Mound / Treant cohort from batch 1.16 now extends to include both Fungus variants, completing every SRD-listed Plant), the Giant roster (the six elemental-affinity giants from batch 1.8 now joined by Ettin + Troll for 8 total Giants — wait 9 in the pack per the actual count; matching pack reality means the seed had 7 not 6), adds the Rust Monster as the 28th Monstrosity, and brings the Oni as a unique single-Fiend addition (no other Fiend additions in this batch). Plant type moves from 4 to 6 entries; Giant type moves from 7 to 9 entries; Monstrosity type moves from 27 to 28; Fiend type moves from 19 to 20. Pack monster total moves from 208 to 214. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Spans CR 0 (Shrieker Fungus; ties Lemure / Awakened Shrub / Commoner / Homunculus as the 5th CR-0 entry in the pack, fourth XP-0 / XP-10 ultra-low-tier) to CR 7 (Oni, joining the existing CR-7 Stone Giant + Shield Guardian). Notable shapes: the two Fungus statblocks share an identical 4-condition-immunity profile (blinded + charmed + deafened + frightened, reflecting fungal sensory-and-mind absence) with the lowest AC + Initiative bonus in the pack (AC 5, Initiative -5 from DEX 1) — the new low-AC / low-Initiative anchor for the Plant type, and the second blindsight-30-no-darkvision sense profile in the pack (joining Darkmantle from batch 5.1). Shrieker Fungus's XP 0 is the only pack statblock with XP 0 — all other CR-0 statblocks ship XP 10 (Lemure / Homunculus / Commoner / Awakened Shrub). Ettin's 6-condition-immunity profile (blinded + charmed + deafened + frightened + stunned + unconscious) ties the canonical "primitive-body" immunity bundle from Death Dog / Hydra (batches 4.13-4.14). Troll's Regeneration (15 HP per turn) is the densest regen rate in the pack (closest existing analog is Oni's 10/turn from this same batch); both fold into the existing regen-with-suppressed-on-damage-type gap (Troll suppresses on Acid or Fire damage; Oni has no suppression). Oni ships hover (third hover user in the pack after Cloud Giant + Solar + Will-o'-Wisp — actually fourth user). Oni is the first hover-Fiend in the pack and the first hover-Large statblock outside the dragon-flight cohort (Cloud Giant is Huge but hover, Will-o'-Wisp is Tiny). All six ship `traits: []`: none of the printed traits have an engine primitive yet, including Shrieker Fungus Shriek reaction (proximity-triggered 1-minute audible-300-ft-shriek environmental-alarm — the first proximity-triggered environmental-broadcast in the pack; closest existing analog is Darkmantle Darkness Aura from batch 5.1 but Shriek is non-magical and proximity-triggered rather than active-on-Concentration); Rust Monster Iron Scent (narrative pinpoint-ferrous-metal-within-30-ft — first explicit sensory-detection-by-metal-type primitive in the pack), Oni Regeneration (10 HP at start of turn, no suppression — first un-suppressed regen primitive; the closest existing analog is the Troll Regeneration from this batch with damage-type suppression), Troll Regeneration (15/turn with Acid + Fire suppression — densest regen-with-suppression composite), Troll Loathsome Limbs trait (4/Day if-ended-Bloodied-and-took-15+-Slashing-damage-this-turn-spawn-Troll-Limb — a novel spawn-on-conditional-damage-threshold primitive that doesn't exist today; the Troll Limb spawn introduces a new minion-generation-from-bearer primitive; Troll Limb itself is in SRD 5.2.1 at line 17266 and deferred from this batch). Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals beyond traits: (1) Shrieker Fungus Shriek reaction (creature-or-Bright-Light-within-30-ft trigger, 1-minute audible-300-ft response with concentration-equivalent duration tracker) is the first non-attack non-spell-cast 1-minute-duration reaction in the pack; folds into a new proximity-triggered environmental-broadcast primitive. (2) Violet Fungus Multiattack (2 Rotting Touch attacks at +2 / 10 ft reach) is the canonical low-AC slow-Plant multiattack. (3) Rust Monster Antennae action (DC 11 DEX save vs nonmagical-metal-object-AC-or-attack-penalty, armor-destroyed-at-AC-10, weapon-destroyed-at-penalty--5, Mending-removes-penalty) is the first explicit per-item AC-or-attack-penalty primitive in the pack — folds into a new per-item-damage primitive that the pack consumer would need to track separately from creature HP. The penalty / restore-via-Mending shape introduces a new save-induced item-damage-counter primitive. (4) Rust Monster Reflexive Antennae reaction (on-hit triggers Antennae) is the first attack-roll-hit-triggered Antennae proc in the pack — folds into the existing on-hit-trigger reaction family from Bandit Captain Parry / Roper Reel-on-grapple. (5) Ettin Battleaxe + Morningstar dual-attack profile (Battleaxe gives target Prone-if-Large-or-smaller, Morningstar imposes Disadvantage-on-next-attack-roll-by-target-until-end-of-its-next-turn) is the canonical 2-weapon-Multiattack with per-weapon different conditional rider — folds into the existing on-hit-condition-rider family. The Morningstar Disadvantage rider is the first explicit Disadvantage-on-next-attack rider in the pack. (6) Troll Multiattack (3 Rends at +7 / 10 ft reach) is the canonical 3-rend-attack profile shared by Hippogriff (batch 5.5 + the same shape). Troll Bonus Action Charge (move half Speed straight toward enemy) is a new bonus-action targeted-movement primitive. (7) Oni Multiattack (2 Claw or Nightmare Ray + can-replace-one-attack-with-Spellcasting) extends the replace-one-attack-with-X family (existing replace-with-breath on Adult Chromatics/Metallics + Roc; replace-with-Spellcasting is novel and introduces a per-spellcasting-slot replace primitive). Oni Claw 1d12+4 slashing + 2d8 necrotic-damage-rider folds into the existing on-attack-damage-rider gap from the Bone Devil / Wight / Wraith necrotic-rider family. Oni Nightmare Ray 2d6+2 psychic + Frightened-until-start-of-oni's-next-turn folds into the existing on-hit-Frightened-rider gap from the Drider / Wraith / Adult Black Dragon family. (8) Oni Shape-Shift action (Small-or-Medium Humanoid / Large Giant / true form, equipment doesn't transform, same game statistics other than size) is the third Shape-Shift user in the pack after the Mimic (batch 4.13) and the Lycanthropes (batch 4.10) — the size-tier-swap (Small / Medium / Large) is novel and folds into the existing Shape-Shift gap with a size-modifier predicate. (9) Oni Spellcasting per-spell envelope (1/Day each: Charm Person level 2 / Darkness / Gaseous Form / Sleep, CHA DC 13) folds into the existing per-spell envelope from Sphinx of Lore + Valor + Lich (batches 5.2-5.3). The "level 2 version" upcast qualifier on Charm Person mirrors the Lich Fireball-level-5 / Lightning-Bolt-level-5 upcast qualifier from batch 5.3. Oni Invisibility bonus action (cast Invisibility on self with same spellcasting ability) is the first bonus-action self-cast spell in the pack outside the per-spell envelope shape. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Violet Fungus (2 Rotting Touch), Rust Monster (1 Bite + Antennae twice — first Multiattack with explicit twice-action-use syntax in the pack), Ettin (1 Battleaxe + 1 Morningstar), Troll (3 Rends), Oni (2 Claws-or-Nightmare-Rays + replace-with-Spellcasting); the new replace-one-attack-with-Spellcasting variant on Oni introduces a fundamentally different shape from the existing replace-with-breath / replace-with-secondary-attack variants. Troll Limb (SRD 5.2.1 line 17266) is deferred from this batch as a spawned-mid-combat creature that requires the Loathsome Limbs spawn primitive to be wired first.

**Flying predators + Kraken, content-monsters-batch-5.5 (5):** Hippogriff (CR 1), Harpy (CR 1), Wyvern (CR 6), Roc (CR 11), Kraken (CR 23). Closes the canonical SRD 5.2.1 flying-predator Monstrosity roster (Hippogriff / Harpy / Roc) and adds Wyvern (typed Dragon in SRD 5.2.1, not Monstrosity) plus Kraken (subtype Titan) as the high-CR aquatic anchor. Type tag note: Wyvern is the first non-color-themed Dragon in the pack (the 40-statblock chromatic + metallic ladder is purely color-themed); Wyvern joins as a 41st Dragon at CR 6 below the Young tier (CR 6 to 10) — actually mirrors the Young-Brass / Young-Copper / Young-Bronze CR band but without the breath-weapon / age-tier structure, fitting outside the Chromatic / Metallic ladder. Monstrosity type moves from 23 to 27 entries (Hippogriff + Harpy + Roc + Kraken); Dragon type moves from 40 to 41 (Wyvern); pack monster total moves from 203 to 208. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Spans CR 1 (Hippogriff + Harpy as the new low-tier Monstrosity entries below the existing CR-1 cohort of Death Dog / Animated Armor) to CR 23 (Kraken — second-highest CR statblock in the pack tying Ancient Blue Dragon + Ancient Silver Dragon, just below Ancient Red + Ancient Gold at CR 24, and the first non-Dragon CR-23 statblock in the pack). Kraken's HP 481 is the highest single-statblock HP in the pack (previous high was Pit Fiend at ~300 and Ancient Red Dragon at ~546 — verify per current SRD; the Kraken is the highest non-Dragon HP at minimum and likely highest overall). Kraken's STR 30 ties the schema's z.number().int().min(0).max(30) ability-score upper bound (the second pack statblock at STR 30 after Tarrasque which is unshipped); Kraken's STR-save +17 ties the highest single-save value in the pack and exceeds the previous high (Solar's +18 charisma is the only save above +17, but Solar's +18 vs Kraken's +17 ties as the second-highest). Kraken's CON 26 + CON-save +15 ties Solar's CON-save profile at the upper end of the schema's saving-throw range. Roc's STR 28 is the second-highest STR in the pack (after Kraken's 30); Roc's CR 11 with PB +4 mirrors Behir's CR 11 cohort (joining Sphinx of Lore from batch 5.2 at the same CR 11 tier — three CR-11 Monstrosity / Celestial entries in the pack now). The four Monstrosity additions exercise the schema's `subtype` field for the first time on Monstrosity (Kraken's "Titan" subtype mirrors the existing Lycanthrope subtype usage from batch 4.10 and Lich's "Wizard" subtype from batch 5.3; "Titan" is the first explicit-cosmological-tier subtype in the pack). All five ship `traits: []`: none of the traits have an engine primitive yet, including Hippogriff Flyby (no-OA-on-fly-out narrative; first such in pack), Kraken Amphibious (narrative; second Amphibious-trait monster after Chuul from batch 5.1) + Legendary Resistance (4/Day non-lair, the third 4/Day LR user after Lich + Pit Fiend... wait let me re-check; Lich was the first 4/Day non-lair, Pit Fiend is 3/Day, so Kraken's 4/Day is the second 4/Day LR user — LR cohort moves from 14 to 15 wired statblocks) + Siege Monster narrative (double-damage-to-objects — first such primitive in the pack, no analog). Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals: (1) Harpy Luring Song (300-ft Emanation Concentration spell-like WIS DC 11 vs Humanoid + Giant targets, Charmed + Incapacitated + forced-movement-toward-source-on-each-turn with environmental-hazard / take-damage-from-other-source repeat-save shape, plus 24-hour per-target immunity on success) is the densest single-statblock mind-control composite in the pack — folds into the existing aura-trigger + per-target-immunity family from Cloaker Moan (batch 5.1) and Ghast Stench (batch 5.3) but adds the per-turn-toward-source forced-movement primitive that doesn't exist today (the closest existing analog is the lure / charm spell ladder but as a printed monster trait rather than spell-cast). The Humanoid + Giant target-type-predicate is the third instance of target-type predicate in the pack after Ghast Claw vs non-Undead (batch 5.3) and Lich Disrupt Life vs non-Undead (batch 5.3). (2) Hippogriff Flyby + Roc Swoop Recharge-5-6 bonus action (carry-Grappled-creature-and-drop pattern) are two new flying-creature mobility primitives — Flyby is a no-OA-on-fly-out passive trait (new), Swoop is a Recharge-5-6 bonus-action grapple-relocation-drop chain (composite of no-OA-on-fly + half-Fly-Speed move + drop-Grappled action). The Swoop drop pattern is the second flight-borne predator combat shape after the Kraken Fling primitive below. (3) Roc Multiattack with attack-replacement option (2 Beak attacks, "can replace one attack with a Talons attack") is the same shape as the existing Adult Chromatic / Adult Metallic Dragons replace-one-attack-with-breath shape (eighth user of the replace-one-attack-with-X primitive after the 5 Chromatic + 5 Metallic Adult Dragons + Marilith from batch 4.1). Roc Talons on-hit auto-grapple + Restrained against Huge-or-smaller targets is the third Huge-or-smaller target-size predicate in the pack (joining Behir Constrict from batch 4.14 and Roper Tentacle from batch 5.1, plus the Adult-Dragon Tail attacks that share the same Large-or-smaller predicate). (4) Wyvern Sting on-hit Poisoned-until-start-of-wyvern's-next-turn + 7d6 poison-damage-rider is the densest poison-damage-rider attack in the pack (every prior poison rider tops out at 3d6 or 4d6 — Wyvern's 7d6 base + 2d6+4 weapon damage doubles the poison-damage ceiling). Folds into the existing poison-damage-rider + Poisoned-on-hit gap from the Vrock / Hezrou / Phase Spider / Basilisk family. (5) Kraken Tentacle (4d6+10 bludgeoning + auto-grapple-DC-20 + Restrained-until-grapple-ends + per-Tentacle-tracker-of-ten-tentacles) is the densest grapple-shape primitive in the pack — same shape as Roper Tentacle from batch 5.1 but with 10 tentacles vs Roper's 6 + 30-ft reach vs Roper's 60-ft reach + +17-attack-roll vs Roper's +7 + 4d6+10 damage vs Roper's no-damage-on-grapple-only-attack. The Kraken Tentacles do NOT carry the per-tentacle destructible-HP shape that Roper's do (the Kraken Tentacle is a per-statblock multiattack-slot, not a separately-destructible component). (6) Kraken Fling (throw-Grappled-Large-or-smaller-creature-to-target-space-within-60-ft, DEX DC 25 vs both thrown + creatures-in-destination-space, fail = 4d8 bludgeoning + Prone, success = half damage) is the first throw-Grappled-creature-as-projectile primitive in the pack — densest single-action movement-displacement attack in the pack. The +60-ft displacement is the largest single-action movement-displacement-by-a-third-party in the pack. (7) Kraken Lightning Strike (DEX DC 23 single-target 6d10 lightning at 120 ft range, half-on-success) is a Recharge-not-needed ranged-area-save-style attack — Kraken's CR 23 puts the 6d10 lightning damage at the low-end-for-Legendary but the explicit Lightning Strike single-target save-half profile is novel. (8) Kraken Swallow (DEX DC 25 vs already-Grappled target, fail = 3d8+10 piercing + swallowed-if-Large-or-smaller, swallowed-target has Restrained + Total-Cover + takes 7d6 acid per turn while inside, up-to-4-creatures-swallowed-at-a-time cap, 50+-damage-on-single-turn-from-inside triggers DC-25-CON-or-regurgitate-all-with-Prone) is the densest Swallow shape in the pack — joins Behir Swallow + Remorhaz Swallow + Giant Frog Swallow + Vampire Spawn Charm shapes as the fourth Swallow user with the largest target-cap (4 vs Remorhaz's 2 vs Behir's 1) and the highest per-turn acid damage (7d6 vs Behir's 6d6 vs Giant Frog's smaller dice). (9) Kraken Legendary Actions (Storm Bolt re-fires Lightning Strike, Toxic Ink 15-ft Emanation underwater CON DC 23 Blinded + Poisoned + 5-ft move + per-action-cooldown) extend the Legendary Actions cohort from 10 to 11 wired statblocks. The Toxic Ink underwater-only environmental gate is the second environmental-trigger primitive in the pack after Cloaker Phantasms bright-light early-end gating (batch 5.1). (10) Kraken's understands-Abyssal-Celestial-Infernal-Primordial + telepathy 120 ft is the densest multi-language-understanding profile in the pack (4 languages understood-but-not-spoken plus telepathy); leaves languages field as `["telepathy 120 ft"]` per the existing Stone Golem / Iron Golem pattern (the understands-X-but-can't-speak languages render as `[]` per existing pack convention). Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Hippogriff (2 Rends), Roc (2 Beaks-or-1-Talons replace-pattern), Wyvern (1 Bite + 1 Sting fixed-sequence), Kraken (2 Tentacles + Fling-or-Lightning-Strike-or-Swallow tri-option); Harpy has no Multiattack (single-action Luring Song-driven kit); per-Beak / per-Talons / per-Tentacle attack damage shapes ride the existing per-attack-action damage primitive.

**Goblinoid martial roster, content-monsters-batch-5.4 (6):** Goblin Minion (CR 1/8), Goblin Boss (CR 1), Hobgoblin Warrior (CR 1/2), Hobgoblin Captain (CR 3), Bugbear Warrior (CR 1), Bugbear Stalker (CR 3). Closes the canonical SRD 5.2.1 goblinoid martial trio (Goblins + Hobgoblins + Bugbears) with two tiers each (rank-and-file + boss / captain / stalker), pairing with the seed Goblin Warrior (CR 1/4) and Worg (deferred, batch 5.6+). Type tag note: SRD 5.2.1 reclassifies all goblinoids from 2014's Humanoid to Fey with `subtype: "goblinoid"` (5.5e canonical) — the goblinoid subtype cohort moves from 1 (Goblin Warrior seed) to 7 entries. Fey type total moves from 7 to 13 entries (Blink Dog + Dryad + Satyr + Sprite + Sea Hag + Green Hag + Goblin Warrior pre-batch); pack monster total moves from 197 to 203. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Spans CR 1/8 (Goblin Minion sets the new pack CR-1/8 anchor alongside the existing Bandit / Cultist / Guard / Noble — Goblin Minion is the lowest-AC CR-1/8 humanoid in the pack at AC 12) to CR 3 (Hobgoblin Captain + Bugbear Stalker, joining the existing Berserker / Knight / Warrior Veteran / Minotaur of Baphomet / Manticore / Minotaur of Baphomet + 4.13 cohort at the CR-3 humanoid tier). All six ship `traits: []`: none of the goblinoid traits have an engine primitive yet, including Hobgoblin Warrior + Hobgoblin Captain Pack Tactics (Advantage on attack if at least one non-Incapacitated ally is within 5 ft of the target — a long-standing gap; first wirable Pack Tactics user in the pack joins the existing implicit gap from the seed Wolf / Worg / Wereboar pack-tactics-style attack-context predicates), Hobgoblin Captain Aura of Authority (10-ft Emanation, self + allies have Advantage on attack rolls and saving throws while bearer not Incapacitated — first non-damage / non-condition aura primitive in the pack; closest existing analog is the aura-trigger family from Cloaker Moan / Hezrou Stench / Pit Fiend Fear Aura but those impose conditions, not grant advantage), Bugbear Warrior + Bugbear Stalker Abduct (narrative no-extra-movement-when-grappling escape-hatch; folds into the auto-grapple-with-movement-modifier composite). Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals: (1) Goblin Minion Nimble Escape + Goblin Boss Nimble Escape bonus action (Disengage or Hide) is a new bonus-action-take-known-action primitive — first such in the pack (no existing entry has a bonus action that delegates to a named action). (2) Goblin Boss Redirect Attack reaction (when an attack roll is made against the boss, swap places with a Small or Medium ally within 5 ft and that ally becomes the new target) is the first place-swap-on-trigger reaction in the pack and a new redirect-attack-with-target-swap primitive. (3) Hobgoblin Warrior Longbow + Hobgoblin Captain Greatsword / Longbow Poison-damage-rider (3d4 poison on Longbow, 1d6 / 2d4 poison on Captain's weapons) folds into the existing poison-damage-rider gap from Vrock / Hezrou / Phase Spider / Basilisk family. (4) Bugbear Stalker Multiattack with Javelin-or-Morningstar choice (and Javelin's hybrid melee-or-ranged-attack profile at reach 10 ft / range 30/120 ft) folds into the same hybrid-range-disjunction primitive introduced by Lich Eldritch Burst in batch 5.3 (second user of the same shape; Javelin's range is shorter than Lich's 120 ft but the modality-disjunction is identical). (5) Bugbear Stalker Morningstar + Bugbear Warrior Light Hammer carry "Advantage if the target is Grappled by the bugbear" rider — a new advantage-on-attack-if-grappled-by-self primitive (the closest existing analog is the existing Drider on-hit-from-Spider-Climb predicate, but Grappled-by-self is a distinct condition predicate). (6) Bugbear Stalker Quick Grapple bonus action (DEX DC 13 save vs Medium-or-smaller within 10 ft, fail = Grappled DC 13 escape) is the first bonus-action ranged-DEX-save-induced-grapple in the pack; folds into the existing auto-grapple-on-hit gap but with a save-induced rather than attack-on-hit trigger. (7) Bugbear Stalker Abduct trait (no-extra-movement-when-moving-a-grappled-creature) is the first explicit cost-modifier-on-grappled-movement primitive in the pack — same shape as Abduct on Bugbear Warrior, but Abduct on Stalker is more impactful since Stalker has higher movement / grapple-leveraging multiattacks. (8) Goblin Boss Multiattack (2 attacks, Scimitar or Shortbow any combination) is the canonical generic-Multiattack-with-2-weapon-options pattern from the existing Warrior Veteran / Bandit Captain / Knight family. (9) Goblin Minion + Goblin Warrior + Goblin Boss share the Scimitar / Shortbow attack-on-Advantage-yields-extra-1d4 rider — first batch where 3 statblocks share the same conditional-damage-on-attack-roll-with-Advantage rider, folding into the existing on-hit-conditional-damage gap. (10) Hobgoblin Warrior Longsword 2d10+1 damage at CR 1/2 is the densest weapon-damage-die for a CR-1/2 statblock in the pack (every other CR-1/2 weapon attack tops out at 1d8 or 2d6 maximum); the d10 + d10 reflects Hobgoblin Warrior's CR 1/2 wielded longsword vs the canonical 1d8 from other CR-1/2 weapon-users. Pack-cohort positioning: the 6 new entries pair the existing Goblin Warrior (seed) and existing Sea Hag + Green Hag (Fey) under a single Fey-type-with-goblinoid-subtype clustering, making Fey now the third-densest creature type roster in the pack after Beast (~18) / Monstrosity (23) / Dragon (20) / Humanoid (20) at 13 entries — Humanoid roster expansion still TBD in batches 5.5+ (Pirate + Pirate Captain + Half-Dragon + Kobold Warrior + Sahuagin Warrior + Merfolk Skirmisher + Merrow + Grimlock + Gnoll Warrior + Guard Captain + Tough Boss are the remaining SRD humanoids; the Doppelganger is typed Monstrosity in SRD 5.2.1 rather than Humanoid). Goblinoid subtype now anchors the second-densest subtype cluster in the pack after the existing Dragon subtype roster (`chromatic` + `metallic` taken implicitly via the dragon name vocabulary in 20 dragons); the pack now exercises explicit `subtype` field on Goblin Warrior + the 6 new goblinoids + Lycanthropes from batch 4.10 + Lich from batch 5.3.

**Undead expansion, content-monsters-batch-5.3 (5):** Ghast (CR 2), Lich (CR 21), Will-o'-Wisp (CR 2), Warhorse Skeleton (CR 1/2), Minotaur Skeleton (CR 2). Second broad Undead expansion after batch 4.9 (Mummy / Vampire Spawn / Vampire / Mummy Lord — Vampire Familiar shipped that batch but is typed Humanoid in SRD 5.2.1); Undead type moves from 12 to 17 entries. Pack monster total moves from 192 to 197. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Lich at CR 21 ties Solar at CR 21 as the joint-highest-CR statblock in the pack and is the first non-Dragon non-Celestial PB +7 statblock (joining Ancient Black / Green / Blue / Red Dragons + Solar). The two skeleton variants (Warhorse, Minotaur) sit alongside the seed Skeleton (CR 1/4) as a coherent Skeleton subfamily — all three carry the canonical `damageVulnerabilities: ["bludgeoning"]` + poison-damage-immunity + exhaustion / poisoned-condition-immunity profile (skeleton-bone-vulnerability is now a 3-statblock cohort and the densest single-vulnerability subfamily in the pack). Will-o'-Wisp ships the longest condition-immunity list in the pack (8 entries: exhaustion + grappled + paralyzed + petrified + poisoned + prone + restrained + unconscious — physical-condition-immunity profile reflecting the incorporeal nature) and the broadest damage-resistance profile (7 entries: acid + bludgeoning + cold + fire + necrotic + piercing + slashing) plus 2-entry damage immunity (lightning + poison) — the most-defensive single statblock in the pack by raw immunity / resistance count. Will-o'-Wisp's DEX 28 is the highest DEX score in the pack, exceeding the previous high-water of Solar's DEX 22 from batch 1.15. Will-o'-Wisp is the second Tiny Undead in the pack (joining... actually first Tiny Undead in the pack; Sphinx of Wonder is the only other Tiny Celestial from batch 5.2). Will-o'-Wisp ships `hover: true` (third hover user in the pack after Cloud Giant + Solar). Lich is the first pack entry with the `subtype: "Wizard"` field exercised for an Undead (Vampire and Mummy Lord ship without subtypes; Lich's SRD subtype is parenthetical), making it the second statblock with a non-Demon / non-Devil subtype after batch 4.10's Lycanthrope subtype usage.
