All five ship `traits: []`: none of the Undead traits in this batch have an engine primitive yet, including Ghast Stench (5-ft Emanation CON DC 10 Poisoned-until-start-of-next-turn with 24-hour per-target immunity on success — folds into the existing aura-trigger + per-target-immunity-after-success family from Cloaker Moan / Hezrou Stench / Balor Fire Aura / Pit Fiend Fear Aura), Lich Legendary Resistance (4/Day non-lair, the second non-Dragon LR user with 4/Day, alongside the existing Adult Chromatic Dragons + Aboleth at 3/Day and Pit Fiend / Balor at 3/Day — LR cohort moves from 13 to 14 wired statblocks; Lich's 4/Day variant exceeds the prior 3/Day cap), Lich Spirit Jar narrative reform-in-1d10-days-if-destroyed (consumer-territory respawn mechanic with no engine analog), Will-o'-Wisp Ephemeral + Illumination + Incorporeal Movement (all narrative: can't-wear / 20-ft-bright-light / move-through-objects-take-1d10-force-damage-if-ends-in-object — Incorporeal Movement is novel in the pack; the closest existing analog is Ghost's Etherealness from batch 1.6 but Ghost ships only the trait label and not the move-through-objects damage shape). Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals beyond traits: (1) Ghast Claw on-hit Paralyzed-CON-DC-10 against non-Undead targets folds into the existing on-hit-save-or-condition gap with a target-type-restricted predicate (the non-Undead qualifier is novel; the closest existing analog is the Lycanthrope-curse-Humanoid-only target predicate from batch 4.10). (2) Warhorse Skeleton + Minotaur Skeleton Trampling Charge composite (moved-20+-feet-straight-toward-target immediately-before-the-hit triggers Prone-on-hit for Warhorse Hooves, extra-2d8-piercing-damage + Prone for Minotaur Gore) is the same shape as the existing Allosaurus / Triceratops / Mammoth / Tyrannosaurus Rex / Wereboar moved-20+-charge family from batches 1.20 and 4.10 — fourth and fifth users of the per-statblock moved-20-feet predicate. (3) Lich Eldritch Burst (melee-or-ranged hybrid attack roll, +12 / reach 5 ft. or range 120 ft.) is the first hybrid-range-modality attack in the pack — every prior attack is strictly melee or strictly ranged. Folds into a new range-disjunction-on-attack primitive. (4) Lich Paralyzing Touch on-hit Paralyzed-until-start-of-lich's-next-turn (no save) is the first guaranteed-condition-on-hit primitive in the pack — every other on-hit condition is gated by a save (Cloaker Attach, Chuul Pincer, Mimic Adhesive). (5) Lich Spellcasting per-spell envelope with At-Will + 2/Day Each + 1/Day Each tier-set folds into the existing per-spell envelope from Sphinx of Lore / Valor in batch 5.2, but the 2/Day Each tier is novel (Sphinx of Lore + Valor + Aboleth + Couatl all use At-Will + 1/Day Each only; Lich's 2/Day Each tier introduces a new spell-uses-tracking primitive variant). Lich casts Detect Magic / Detect Thoughts / Dispel Magic / Fireball (level 5 version) / Invisibility / Lightning Bolt (level 5 version) / Mage Hand / Prestidigitation at-will + Animate Dead / Dimension Door / Plane Shift 2/Day each + Chain Lightning / Finger of Death / Power Word Kill / Scrying 1/Day each, using INT (DC 20). The "level 5 version" upcast-at-monster-casting-tier qualifier on Fireball / Lightning Bolt is a new permanent-upcast-spell-as-monster-action primitive variant. (6) Lich Protective Magic reaction (casts Counterspell or Shield as reaction to a spell trigger) folds into the existing reaction-cast-spell shape; Counterspell + Shield are both reaction-spells in the pack. (7) Lich Legendary Actions (Deathly Teleport 60-ft self-teleport with 10-ft 2d10 necrotic AoE around the departure point — novel "AoE around departure point" shape that doesn't exist today; Disrupt Life 20-ft Emanation CON DC 20, 9d6 necrotic vs. non-Undead, with the existing "can't take this action again until start of next turn" per-action-cooldown shape; Frightening Gaze casts Fear with per-action cooldown) extends the Legendary Actions cohort from 9 to 10 wired statblocks (Aboleth + 5 Adult Chromatics + Pit Fiend + Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor + Lich). The Disrupt Life "creature that isn't an Undead" target-type-exclusion is a second-instance of the target-type-predicate primitive from Ghast Claw. (8) Will-o'-Wisp Consume Life (bonus action CON DC 10 against living creature within 5 ft with 0 HP, fail = target dies + wisp regains 3d6 HP) is the first execute-at-0-HP primitive in the pack and folds into the dying / unconscious / stable resolution family with a novel target-must-have-0-HP precondition. (9) Will-o'-Wisp Vanish (bonus action Concentration Invisible until attack roll or Consume Life ends it) folds into the existing Invisibility + Concentration gap with a novel self-cancel-on-attack-roll-or-self-action exit predicate. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Lich (3 attacks: Eldritch Burst or Paralyzing Touch in any combination — same shape as the Marilith 6-Pact-Blade-attack from batch 4.1 and Lich's three-of-two-options shape introduces the same "choose-from-N-attack-types-per-Multiattack" shape; Ghast's two-action profile is Bite + Claw, not flagged Multiattack — first Undead in the pack with two separate action options but no Multiattack tag, requiring per-statblock action-economy guidance the engine doesn't surface today; Warhorse + Minotaur Skeleton single-attack Multiattack-implicit shape mirrors the existing Beast cohort).

**Construct + Sphinx cohort, content-monsters-batch-5.2 (6):** Clay Golem (CR 9), Flesh Golem (CR 5), Homunculus (CR 0); Sphinx of Wonder (CR 1), Sphinx of Lore (CR 11), Sphinx of Valor (CR 17). Closes the SRD 5.2.1 Golem family (Stone + Iron already in pack from batch 1.12) and opens the Sphinx subfamily under Celestial. Construct type moves from 6 to 9 entries; Celestial type moves from 6 to 9 entries (the Sphinx trio expands the slice-1.15 angel-roster + Pegasus / Couatl / Unicorn coverage). Pack monster total moves from 186 to 192. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Spans CR 0 (Homunculus, the new pack CR-0 anchor for Construct — Awakened Shrub from batch 1.16 remains the Plant CR-0 entry and Lemure from batch 1.7 remains the Fiend CR-0 entry) to CR 17 (Sphinx of Valor, third-highest CR Celestial after Solar at 21 and Planetar at 16, and now the second-highest CR statblock outside the Adult / Ancient Dragon + Solar tier). Magic Resistance is wired on Clay Golem, Flesh Golem, and Sphinx of Wonder via `GrantMagicResistance` (slice-131 cohort moves from 30 to 33 wired users); the two large Sphinxes (Lore, Valor) carry Inscrutable + Legendary Resistance instead of Magic Resistance per SRD 5.2.1 and ship `traits: []` since neither primitive is engine-supported yet. Sphinx of Valor's PB +6 with a four-save proficiency profile (DEX +6, CON +11, INT +9, WIS +12) is the densest saving-throw spread in the pack outside the Ancient Chromatic Dragons (slice-130 fast-path now exercised by every non-Dragon CR-17+ statblock too). Sphinx of Valor's WIS save +12 ties the highest in the pack (Solar's WIS save also +12 at PB +7) and exercises the upper end of the schema's saving-throw range. Damage profile highlights: Clay Golem carries B/P/S resistance straight in `damageResistances` (no qualifier — SRD 5.2.1 dropped the "not adamantine" rider that Iron Golem still carries; pack Iron Golem leaves B/P/S off entirely, matching SRD), plus acid / poison / psychic immunity and the canonical 6-condition Golem immunity bundle (charmed / exhaustion / frightened / paralyzed / petrified / poisoned, same as Stone + Iron Golem). Flesh Golem carries lightning + poison damage immunity (lightning is novel to the Golem family — Stone has none, Iron has fire / poison / psychic, Clay has acid / poison / psychic) and the same 6-condition Golem bundle. Homunculus carries the lightest condition-immunity profile of any Construct in the pack (charmed + poisoned only) and is the third Tiny Construct in the pack (joining... actually first Tiny Construct in the pack; the existing Sphinx of Wonder below is Tiny Celestial). Sphinx of Wonder is the first Tiny Celestial and the second Tiny entry in this batch (with Homunculus); both share Tiny size + fly 40 + darkvision 60. Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor share truesight 120 (joining Couatl + Deva / Planetar / Solar from batch 1.15) as the Celestial canonical sense profile. Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals beyond the wired `GrantMagicResistance` traits: (1) Clay Golem Acid Absorption (heals HP equal to acid damage dealt — first heal-from-damage-type-instead-of-take-damage mechanic in the pack; closest existing analog is Flesh Golem Lightning Absorption from this same batch and a future engine primitive that doesn't yet exist), and Flesh Golem Lightning Absorption (identical shape for lightning damage). Both fold into a new heal-on-incoming-damage-type primitive that joins the existing damage-resistance / immunity vocabulary. (2) Clay Golem + Flesh Golem Berserk trait (start-of-turn-while-Bloodied, 1d6 = 6 triggers berserk mode targeting nearest creature) is the first Bloodied-trigger conditional behavior modifier in the pack; folds into a new bloodied-state-trigger primitive that doesn't exist today. Flesh Golem's variant adds a creator-DC-15-CHA-Persuasion-check-to-calm sub-mechanic that introduces a per-creature-relationship calm-via-check shape. (3) Clay Golem + Flesh Golem Immutable Form trait (can't shape-shift) is narrative under the existing Shape-Shift gap (Vampire / Mummy Lord / Lycanthropes / Hag / Genie / Mimic family). (4) Clay Golem Slam HP-max-decrease-on-acid-damage rider folds into the existing Mummy / Mummy Lord / Vampire Familiar HP-max-decay family from batches 4.9 and 5.1. (5) Clay Golem Hasten (Recharge 5-6 bonus action: Dash + Disengage) is the first Recharge-5-6 bonus-action mechanic in the pack — the slice-140 breath weapon primitive handles Recharge-5-6 area saves but bonus-action self-buff Recharge is a distinct primitive shape. (6) Flesh Golem Aversion to Fire (Disadvantage on attacks + ability checks until end of next turn if hit by fire damage) is the first take-damage-type-imposes-Disadvantage-rider in the pack; folds into a new on-damage-type-imposed-condition primitive (the Disadvantage condition is unnamed today). (7) Homunculus Bite Poisoned + Unconscious-while-Poisoned (CON DC 12 on hit, with a Failure-by-5-or-More escalation extending the duration from "until end of homunculus's next turn" to "1 minute") is the second Failure-by-5-or-More escalation primitive in the pack after the existing Vampire Bite mechanic family from batch 4.9. The Unconscious-while-Poisoned compound condition is the same shape as Chuul's Paralyzed-while-Poisoned (batch 5.1). (8) Homunculus Telepathic Bond trait (same-plane bidirectional telepathy with master) is narrative; closest existing analog is the angel-cohort telepathy 120 ft from batch 1.15. (9) Sphinx of Wonder Burst of Ingenuity reaction (2/Day, +2 to ability check or save by self or creature within 30 ft) is a new reaction-augments-roll primitive — the closest existing analog is Bardic Inspiration's reactive +d-roll bonus, but Sphinx of Wonder's is a fixed +2 with a reaction trigger condition. (10) Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor Inscrutable trait (remote-observation + thought-detection prohibition + Disadvantage on Insight-to-ascertain-intent checks) is a new sense-blocking + check-Disadvantage composite primitive. (11) Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor Legendary Resistance (3/Day, or 4/Day in Lair — pack ships non-lair only) is the existing Legendary Resistance primitive from the Adult Chromatic / Adult Metallic / Aboleth cohort (cohort moves from 11 to 13 LR users; Pit Fiend + Balor + Marilith already carry it from batches 4.1-4.2). (12) Sphinx of Lore Mind-Rending Roar (Recharge 5-6, 300-ft Emanation WIS DC 16, 10d6 psychic + Incapacitated until start of next turn) is a new Recharge-5-6 area-save-and-condition mechanic; folds into the slice-140 breath weapon primitive shape with an added condition rider (Incapacitated). The 300-ft Emanation is the second-largest area in the pack after Sphinx of Valor's 500-ft Roar emanation below. (13) Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor Spellcasting (per-spell envelope: at-will + 1/Day Each lists) folds into the existing per-spell-envelope innate spellcasting deferral from batches 1.4 (Mage / Druid / Priest), 1.14 (Dryad), and 1.15 (Couatl). Sphinx of Lore casts Detect Magic / Identify / Mage Hand / Minor Illusion / Prestidigitation at will + Dispel Magic / Legend Lore / Locate Object / Plane Shift / Remove Curse / Tongues 1/Day each, using INT (DC 16). Sphinx of Valor casts Detect Evil and Good / Thaumaturgy at will + Detect Magic / Dispel Magic / Greater Restoration / Heroes' Feast / Zone of Truth 1/Day each, using WIS (DC 20). The DC 20 spell-save matches Sphinx of Valor's overall save DC tier and is the third-highest spell-save-DC in the pack (after Solar at 25 and Ancient Red Dragon Frightful Presence at 21). (14) Sphinx of Valor Roar (3/Day with a three-stage sequence per Long Rest: First Roar = Frightened 1 minute, Second Roar = Paralyzed with repeated end-of-turn saves capped at 1 minute, Third Roar = 8d10 thunder + Prone with half-on-success) is a new sequenced-uses-with-different-effects primitive — first such shape in the pack. The 500-ft Emanation is the largest area-of-effect in the pack to date (previously the 300-ft Sphinx of Lore roar). (15) Sphinx of Lore + Sphinx of Valor Legendary Actions (Arcane Prowl 30-ft teleport + Claw, Weight of Years CON DC 16 — Sphinx of Lore — / DC 20 — Sphinx of Valor — Exhaustion-level-grant + 3d10-years-aging-appearance composite) extend the existing Legendary Actions cohort from 7 to 9 users (Aboleth + 5 Adult Chromatics + Pit Fiend prior). Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Clay Golem (2 Slams or 3 Slams if Hasten used this turn — first Multiattack-count-conditional-on-prior-action primitive in the pack), Flesh Golem (2 Slams), Sphinx of Lore (3 Claws), Sphinx of Valor (2 Claws + Roar — first Multiattack including a Roar-class non-attack action since the Chimera-Ram + Bite + Claw + Fire-Breath shape in batch 4.14); Sphinx of Lore Mind-Rending Roar + Sphinx of Valor Roar fold into the slice-140 breath weapon primitive shape but ship as `breathWeapon: undefined` since neither is a damage-only area save (Mind-Rending Roar adds Incapacitated, Sphinx of Valor's Roar adds Frightened / Paralyzed / Prone depending on roar count); Clay Golem Acid Absorption + Flesh Golem Lightning Absorption fold into a new heal-on-damage-type primitive; Clay Golem + Flesh Golem Berserk Bloodied-trigger folds into a new Bloodied-state primitive; Homunculus Bite Failure-by-5-or-More escalation reuses the slice-148 Vampire Bite shape.

**Aberration sweep, content-monsters-batch-5.1 (5):** Chuul (CR 4), Cloaker (CR 8), Darkmantle (CR 1/2), Grick (CR 2), Roper (CR 5). Closes the SRD 5.2.1 Aberration roster outside the seed Aboleth / Gibbering Mouther / Otyugh; Aberration type moves from 3 to 8 entries (the type's first broad expansion since batch 1.13 opened the type). Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Pack monster total moves from 181 to 186. Spans CR 1/2 to 8; Darkmantle sets the new Aberration CR floor below the existing Gibbering Mouther / Otyugh / Aboleth tier and is the second blindsight-60-with-no-darkvision sense profile in the pack (joining Black Pudding from batch 1.11). All five ship `traits: []`: none of the printed traits have an engine primitive yet, including Chuul Amphibious + Sense Magic (passive Detect Magic in 120-ft sphere, no save / no DC, new innate-detection narrative shape), Cloaker Light Sensitivity (Disadvantage on attack rolls in bright light, folds into the Shadow / Wight / Specter / Drider sunlight-sensitivity family as a fifth user with the bright-light-vs-sunlight distinction unhandled today), and Roper Spider Climb (narrative, same shape as the Phase Spider Web Walker / Giant Spider Spider Climb / Drider Spider Climb gap, fourth user). Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals beyond traits: (1) auto-grapple-on-hit appears on Chuul Pincer (DC 14, Large-or-smaller), Grick Tentacles (DC 12, Medium-or-smaller, all four tentacles), and Roper Tentacle (DC 14, six destructible tentacles), three users of the existing auto-grapple-on-hit gap. (2) Chuul Paralyzing Tentacles is a target-already-Grappled CON DC 13 save that escalates Poisoned then Paralyzed-while-Poisoned with a per-turn-end save and a 1-minute auto-success cap, folding into the two-tier condition escalation gap with a new compound-condition predicate (Paralyzed gated on Poisoned). (3) Cloaker Attach (DC 14 STR Athletics escape, attached-target-Blinded, attached-target-takes-shared-damage-when-cloaker-damaged) is the first explicit damage-share-on-attach mechanic in the pack; Mimic Adhesive (batch 4.13) is the closest existing shape but shares no damage. (4) Cloaker Phantasms (Recharge after Short or Long Rest casts Mirror Image using WIS as the spellcasting ability) folds into the existing Recharge-per-rest spell-cast gap, with bright-light early-end gating introducing a per-spell-trigger environmental termination predicate. (5) Cloaker Moan (60-ft Emanation WIS DC 13, Frightened until end of cloaker's next turn, 24-hour per-target immunity on success) folds into the aura-trigger + per-target-immunity-after-success family with the existing Balor / Pit Fiend / Hezrou Stench aura shape, but adds the per-target-24-hour-immunity tracker. (6) Darkmantle Crush auto-attach + Blinded + suffocating + speed-0-on-attach + advantage-attacked-only-this-target (DC 13 STR Athletics escape) is the densest single-attack-attach in the pack; folds into the Mimic Adhesive shape with an additional cover-target-fully-on-Medium-or-smaller branch and the auto-Blinded + suffocating composite. (7) Darkmantle Darkness Aura (1/Day Concentration 15-ft Emanation magical darkness with Darkvision-penetration-suppression) is the first emanation-Concentration-magical-darkness in the pack; the closest existing analog is the cross-aura family from Balor / Hezrou / Pit Fiend but applied as an environment modifier rather than damage / condition emanation. (8) Roper Reel pull-Grappled-target-30-ft-toward-roper is the first directional-movement-on-Grappled mechanic in the pack; Behir Constrict (batch 4.14) is the closest existing shape but with no movement clause. (9) Roper Tentacle destructible-tentacle composite (six tentacles, each AC 20 / HP 10 / immune-to-poison-and-psychic / regrow-at-start-of-next-turn) is the densest per-attack-slot destructible-component primitive in the pack; Hydra's per-head tracker from batch 4.14 is the closest existing analog (per-head HP tracker + regrow rule), but Roper's tentacles are bound to a specific attack rather than the whole-creature multiattack-count tracker. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Chuul (2 Pincers + Paralyzing Tentacles), Cloaker (1 Attach + 2 Tails), Grick (Beak + Tentacles), and Roper (2 Tentacles + Reel + 2 Bites); four of five Aberrations in this batch have Multiattack, leaving Darkmantle as the only single-attack-only Aberration in the batch. Auto-Poisoned-until-grapple-ends on Roper Tentacle and the Poisoned-then-Paralyzed chain on Chuul are the first non-damage poison-condition appearances in the Aberration roster.

**MM beasts (6):** Goblin Warrior (CR 1/4; renamed from Goblin in slice 142), Wolf (CR 1/4), Skeleton (CR 1/4), Ogre (CR 2), Young Red Dragon (CR 10), and one entry (Orc) since dropped in slice 141 (Orc removed from SRD 5.2.1 monster catalog).

**NPC roster, content-monsters-batch-1.1 (10):** Bandit (CR 1/8), Bandit Captain (CR 2), Cultist (CR 1/8), Cult Fanatic (CR 2; renamed to Cultist Fanatic in slice 142), Acolyte (CR 1/4; renamed to Priest Acolyte in slice 142), Commoner (CR 0), Guard (CR 1/8), Noble (CR 1/8), Scout (CR 1/2), Spy (CR 1).

**NPC roster, content-monsters-batch-1.2 (5):** Tribal Warrior (CR 1/8; renamed to Warrior Infantry in slice 142), Thug (CR 1/2; renamed to Tough in slice 142), Berserker (CR 2), Veteran (CR 3; renamed to Warrior Veteran in slice 142), Knight (CR 3). Closes the humanoid roster up through CR 3.

**Bestiary, content-monsters-batch-1.3 (8):** Zombie (CR 1/4), Ghoul (CR 1), Giant Rat (CR 1/8), Giant Spider (CR 1), Giant Wolf Spider (CR 1/4), Brown Bear (CR 1), Dire Wolf (CR 1), Stirge (CR 1/8). First broad fill outside humanoids: 6 Beasts + 2 Undead, covering the most-encountered low-CR creature types.

**Caster NPCs, content-monsters-batch-1.4 (originally 4, now 3 after slice 141):** Priest (CR 2), Druid (CR 2), Mage (CR 6). Apprentice Wizard dropped in slice 141 (not in SRD 5.2.1). Closes the spell-using humanoid NPC gap. All three hit the existing monster-spellcasting deferral (no new primitive needed to wire if monster spellcasting ever lands).

**Bestiary tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.5 (6):** Mastiff (CR 1/8), Boar (CR 1/4), Constrictor Snake (CR 1/4), Giant Frog (CR 1/4), Giant Centipede (CR 1/4), Black Bear (CR 1/2). Fills the low-CR Beast pile out to encounter-table density for wilderness / dungeon ambient threats.

**Low-CR Undead variety, content-monsters-batch-1.6 (5):** Shadow (CR 1/2), Specter (CR 1), Wight (CR 3), Ghost (CR 4), Wraith (CR 5). Fills the Undead pile out to a usable haunted-location roster. First batch to populate `traits` on monster statblocks: all five carry `GrantResistance` entries with `qualifier: 'nonmagical'` for B/P/S (slice 112 effect shape). This data is currently inert at runtime (see the cross-cutting structural-gap note below), but ships RAW-accurate so it wires for free when the engine consumes monster data.

**Low-CR Fiend introduction, content-monsters-batch-1.7 (originally 5, now 4 after slice 141):** Lemure (CR 0), Dretch (CR 1/4), Imp (CR 1), Quasit (CR 1). Manes dropped in slice 141 (not in SRD 5.2.1). Opens the Fiend creature type with the canonical low-tier demons and devils, including the familiar pair (Imp / Quasit). Three of the four (Imp, Lemure, Quasit) carry the slice-112 `GrantResistance` B/P/S nonmagical traits; Imp and Lemure's RAW "not made with silvered weapons" further qualifier is deferred (same gap as Wight in batch 1.6). Subtype field exercised for the first time (`subtype: "devil"`, `"demon"`, `"devil, shapechanger"`, `"demon, shapechanger"`).

**Giant cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.8 (6):** Hill Giant (CR 5), Stone Giant (CR 7), Frost Giant (CR 8), Fire Giant (CR 9), Cloud Giant (CR 9), Storm Giant (CR 13). Opens the Giant creature type with the canonical six elemental-affinity giants, covering CR 5-13 as a single coherent set. Exercises damage immunities (Frost: cold; Fire: fire; Storm: lightning + thunder), damage resistances (Storm: cold), and the full save / skill / sense kit on every entry. First time the pack carries a CR 13 statblock. All six ship `traits: []` pending Multiattack / monster-action vocabulary; the elemental-affinity damage-modifier data is RAW-accurate and will wire for free when the engine consumes `monster.damageImmunities` / `damageResistances` (see cross-cutting structural-gap note below).

**Elemental cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.9 (5):** Air Elemental (CR 5), Earth Elemental (CR 5), Fire Elemental (CR 5), Water Elemental (CR 5), Invisible Stalker (CR 6). Opens the Elemental creature type with all four base elementals plus the Invisible Stalker as the canonical CR 6 air-elemental variant. Every entry carries the slice-112 `GrantResistance` B/P/S nonmagical traits, plus elemental-affinity damage modifiers: Air resists lightning / thunder; Earth takes thunder vulnerability (first new vulnerability entry beyond the seed Skeleton's bludgeoning); Fire is immune to fire; Water resists acid. Every entry is immune to poison and to a near-complete suite of physical-state conditions (exhaustion, grappled, paralyzed, petrified, poisoned, prone, restrained, unconscious). First time `damageVulnerabilities` is populated post-seed and first time `tremorsense` appears (Earth Elemental 60 ft).

**Monstrosity opener, content-monsters-batch-1.10 (6):** Ankheg (CR 2), Bulette (CR 5), Griffon (CR 2), Manticore (CR 3), Minotaur (CR 3), Owlbear (CR 3). Opens the Monstrosity creature type with six adventure-staple iconic creatures in the CR 2-5 sweet spot (the underrepresented wilderness / dungeon middle band of the pack). All six ship as bare statblocks (`traits: []`) pending Multiattack and the on-hit save / damage rider primitives. Three of six carry the burrow / fly / tremorsense speed and sense kit (Ankheg, Bulette, Griffon). Languages: only Manticore (Common) and Minotaur (Abyssal) speak.

**Ooze cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.11 (4):** Black Pudding (CR 4), Gelatinous Cube (CR 2), Gray Ooze (CR 1/2), Ochre Jelly (CR 2). Closes the Ooze creature type with the canonical four. Every entry shares a tight mechanical pattern: blindsight 60 (blind beyond), the full ooze condition-immunity profile (blinded, charmed, deafened, exhaustion, frightened, prone), Amorphous movement (deferred under the existing narrative-movement note), and a Pseudopod attack with acid damage. Damage profiles diverge by type: Black Pudding (immune acid / cold / lightning / slashing), Gelatinous Cube (no resistances or immunities), Gray Ooze (resist acid / cold / fire), Ochre Jelly (resist acid; immune lightning / slashing). First time the pack carries `damageImmunities: ["slashing"]` (Black Pudding, Ochre Jelly) and `damageImmunities: ["lightning"]`. All four ship `traits: []`.

**Construct ladder, content-monsters-batch-1.12 (6):** Animated Armor (CR 1), Flying Sword (CR 1/4; renamed to Animated Flying Sword in slice 142), Rug of Smothering (CR 2; renamed to Animated Rug of Smothering in slice 142), Shield Guardian (CR 7), Stone Golem (CR 10), Iron Golem (CR 16). Opens the Construct creature type across a wide CR 1/4-16 band; first time the pack carries a CR 16 statblock. The three low-tier constructs (Animated Armor, Animated Flying Sword, Animated Rug of Smothering) share the canonical "animated object" condition-immunity suite (blinded, charmed, deafened, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, petrified, poisoned) plus poison and psychic damage immunity and blindsight 60 (blind beyond). The two Golems carry slice-112 `GrantResistance` B/P/S nonmagical traits (RAW: "not adamantine" further qualifier deferred, same gap as Wight's silvered qualifier in batch 1.6) plus poison / psychic immunity and an expanded condition-immunity profile (no blinded / deafened, gains petrified). Iron Golem also has fire immunity, healing from fire damage deferred separately. The Animated Rug of Smothering's slashing vulnerability is the second post-seed `damageVulnerabilities` entry (joining Earth Elemental's thunder).

**Aberration opener, content-monsters-batch-1.13 (originally 5, now 3 after slice 141):** Aboleth (CR 10), Gibbering Mouther (CR 2), Otyugh (CR 5). Beholder and Mind Flayer dropped in slice 141 (WotC trademarks, never in any SRD). Opened the Aberration creature type. Aboleth carries telepathy as a `languages` array entry pending a proper directional-sense / language-vs-sense schema split; Otyugh carries its single fictional language `otyugh` with "limited telepathy" deferred separately. Gibbering Mouther is immune to the prone condition (the amorphous biology). All three ship `traits: []`. Original batch-1.13 deferral-discovery footprint, now narrower since Beholder + Mind Flayer dropped: still opens Legendary Actions and Legendary Resistance (now via Aboleth alone in this batch; Adult Chromatics in batch 1.18 broadened the user list), Enslave with recurring save (Aboleth, same shape as Quasit Scare), and a half-dozen narrative riders. Antimagic Cone, Eye Rays, Mind Blast, Tentacle stun on grapple, and Extract Brain were Beholder/Mind-Flayer-only deferrals; they're dropped from the queue now that their canonical users are gone.

**Fey cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.14 (originally 5, now 4 after slice 141):** Blink Dog (CR 1/4), Dryad (CR 1), Satyr (CR 1/2), Sprite (CR 1/4). Pixie dropped in slice 141 (not in SRD 5.2.1). Opens the Fey creature type with the canonical low-CR roster. Two of four (Dryad, Satyr) carry Magic Resistance, folded into the existing entry. Dryad carries a per-spell envelope innate spellcasting list (Druid casting flavor); Couatl in batch 1.15 is now the densest single-monster spell list in the pack at 13 entries. All four ship `traits: []`.

**Celestial cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.15 (6):** Pegasus (CR 2), Couatl (CR 4), Unicorn (CR 5), Deva (CR 10), Planetar (CR 16), Solar (CR 21). Opens the Celestial creature type across the widest CR band yet — Solar at CR 21 is the highest-CR statblock in the pack (previously Iron Golem at 16). The four angels (Couatl, Deva, Planetar, Solar) carry slice-112 `GrantResistance` B/P/S nonmagical traits plus radiant resistance and condition-immunity profiles canonical to Celestials (charmed / exhaustion / frightened, plus poison-immunity on Solar). Couatl ships truesight 120 (first time the senses field exercises this key) and `all languages` + telepathy 120 ft (the angels share this language profile). Solar carries the highest XP in the pack (33000) and the highest proficiency bonus (+7). Pegasus and Unicorn ship `traits: []`; the four angels populate the standard B/P/S nonmagical resistance traits.

**Plant cohort, content-monsters-batch-1.16 (4):** Awakened Shrub (CR 0), Awakened Tree (CR 2), Shambling Mound (CR 5), Treant (CR 9). Closes the Plant creature type with the canonical SRD four, completing every MM creature type that has SRD-licensed entries (the pack now covers every creature type at least once). Three of four (Awakened Shrub, Awakened Tree, Treant) ship `damageVulnerabilities: ["fire"]` — the largest single-batch population of the vulnerability field and the third-through-fifth post-seed entries (joining Skeleton's bludgeoning, Earth Elemental's thunder, Animated Rug of Smothering's slashing). Three of four also carry plain (unqualified) `damageResistances` for bludgeoning / piercing rather than the slice-112 `GrantResistance.qualifier` form, since RAW Plant resistance is unconditional, not source-qualified. Shambling Mound exercises lightning immunity (with Lightning Absorption healing deferred separately) plus cold / fire resistance and blindsight 60. All four ship `traits: []`.

**Young Chromatic Dragon tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.17 (4):** Young White Dragon (CR 6), Young Black Dragon (CR 7), Young Green Dragon (CR 8), Young Blue Dragon (CR 9). First tier-up-within-existing-type batch (every prior content batch opened a new type or expanded the humanoid roster). Closes the Young Chromatic Dragon set started by the seed's Young Red Dragon at CR 10, mirroring its statblock shape: Large Dragon, blindsight 30 + darkvision 120, expertise on Perception, multi-mode speed (each color has its own walk / burrow / fly / swim mix appropriate to its environment), Common + Draconic. Each ships its canonical elemental immunity (cold / acid / poison / lightning). Young Green also adds the poisoned condition immunity (the only Young Chromatic with one). All four ship `traits: []`. The pack now reaches one hundred statblocks (round-number milestone).

**Adult Chromatic Dragon tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.18 (5):** Adult White Dragon (CR 13), Adult Black Dragon (CR 14), Adult Green Dragon (CR 15), Adult Blue Dragon (CR 16), Adult Red Dragon (CR 17). Closes the entire chromatic Adult Dragon ladder in a single batch. Each is Huge size, blindsight 60 + darkvision 120, expertise on Perception, canonical elemental immunity, and Common + Draconic. Adult Green additionally gains poisoned condition immunity. The cohort introduces the first batch where every entry uses Legendary Actions and Legendary Resistance (3/day each) and exercises Frightful Presence (a new mechanic-level deferral introduced this batch). Adult Red's proficiency bonus +6 is the second-highest in the pack (after Solar's +7). The five Adult Chromatics share an exact statblock template with Adult White / Black / Green / Blue / Red scaling parameterized only by CR, ability scores, breath shape / DC / dice, bite-rider die, and Frightful Presence DC — making them the highest-density per-data tier-up in the pack so far.

**Devil ladder tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.19 (originally 5, now 4 after slice 141):** Bearded Devil (CR 3), Barbed Devil (CR 5), Chain Devil (CR 8), Bone Devil (CR 9). Spined Devil dropped in slice 141 (not in SRD 5.2.1). Closes the mid-tier Devil hierarchy started by Imp (CR 1) and Lemure (CR 0) in batch 1.7. All four share the canonical Devil damage profile (cold resistance, fire / poison immunity, B/P/S nonmagical resistance via slice-112 `GrantResistance` traits with the "not silvered" further qualifier deferred per the established Wight / Imp gap, poisoned condition immunity, darkvision 120, Infernal + telepathy 120 ft, Magic Resistance, Devil's Sight). The Bone Devil is the first Large devil in the pack (joining the existing low-tier Tiny / Small / Medium fiends). Each carries a distinctive signature action that surfaces a new mechanic-level deferral.

**Beast megafauna tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.20 (6):** Pteranodon (CR 1/4), Plesiosaurus (CR 2), Allosaurus (CR 2), Triceratops (CR 5), Mammoth (CR 6), Tyrannosaurus Rex (CR 8). Closes the high-CR Beast gap with the canonical SRD dinosaurs (Pteranodon, Plesiosaurus, Allosaurus, Triceratops, T-Rex) plus Mammoth as the prehistoric-megafauna companion. Beast cohort prior to this batch capped at Brown Bear / Dire Wolf at CR 1; the pack now ranges through CR 8 in Beasts. Tyrannosaurus Rex is the first Beast with Multiattack. All six ship `traits: []`. Three of six (Allosaurus Pounce, Triceratops Trampling Charge, Mammoth Trampling Charge) extend the existing Charge deferral; T-Rex's bite-auto-grapple with restricted-target-of-bite folds into the existing Ankheg-shaped auto-grapple gap.

**Humanoid combat tier-up, content-monsters-batch-1.21 (2):** Gladiator (CR 5), Assassin (CR 8). Closes the humanoid combat tier-up gap explicitly called out in the gap-notes tail. Both ship `traits: []`. The Gladiator extends the Bandit Captain / Knight / Warrior Veteran / Berserker / Tough humanoid combatant ladder up through CR 5 with three-attack Multiattack, Parry reaction, and shield-bash-with-prone; the Assassin closes the high-CR humanoid rogue-archetype slot with Sneak Attack, Evasion, Assassinate, and poisoned weapon attacks. Both notable for borrowing extensive class-feature shapes (Brave / Parry / Sneak Attack / Evasion / Cunning Action exist as class features; the monster-borrow pathway is the established deferral). One new mechanic-level deferral: Assassinate (composite of first-turn-vs-uninitiated-target advantage + auto-crit-on-surprised target).

**Mid-tier Monstrosity sweep, content-monsters-batch-4.14 (6):** Chimera (CR 6), Drider (CR 6), Medusa (CR 6), Hydra (CR 8), Behir (CR 11), Remorhaz (CR 11). Extends the Monstrosity ladder from the batch-4.13 low-tier sweep into the mid-to-upper-mid tier (CR 6 to 11). The Monstrosity roster moves from 17 to 23 entries (Beast at ~18 remains the largest pack roster outside the Dragon ladder, then Monstrosity at 23, then Humanoid at 20). Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Type-tagging note: SRD 5.2.1 reclassified several traditionally-Monstrosity creatures (Gorgon → Construct, Troll → Giant, Lamia → Fiend, Roper → Aberration); the batch ships only entries SRD-typed as Monstrosity. Pack monster total moves from 175 to 181. Cohort highlights: Behir's CR 11 with 168 HP + lightning immunity + draconic language + Lightning Breath (90-ft line, DEX DC 16, 12d10) is the first non-Dragon Lightning Breath user in the pack and folds cleanly into the slice-140 breath weapon primitive — but the batch ships `traits: []` on Behir as a coherence choice (the breath weapon is an action rather than a baseline trait; wiring would mirror the dragon-tier breath wiring but is deferred under the dragon-vs-monstrosity breath-weapon-coherence question). Chimera's three-headed Multiattack (Ram + Bite + Claw, with Claw-replaceable-by-Fire-Breath) is the first three-flavor-per-multiattack monster (the existing Adult Chromatic Dragons + Adult Metallics replace-one-attack-with-secondary-breath shape; Chimera is the first multi-flavor variant where each "head" has its own attack type) — exercises the same multiattack-with-options sub-shape as the Metallic Dragons but with three distinct attack flavors rather than weapon-plus-breath-swap. Chimera Bite advantage-on-hit-becomes-4d6+4 introduces the first "if-attack-had-advantage-doubled-damage" rider in the pack — folds into the on-hit-conditional-damage gap with a new advantage-source predicate. Chimera Ram's prone-on-hit-against-Medium-or-smaller folds into the existing on-hit-save-or-condition gap (size-conditional prone). Chimera Fire Breath (Recharge 5-6, 15-ft cone, DEX DC 15, 7d8) is a dragon-style breath on a non-Dragon — same shape as the slice-140 primitive, deferred for now under the dragon-vs-monstrosity-breath coherence question. Drider's Foreleg + Poison Burst attacks (melee + ranged variants per Multiattack), Magic of the Spider Queen (Recharge 5-6 spell-cast Darkness / Faerie Fire / Web at WIS DC 14), Spider Climb (narrative), Sunlight Sensitivity (Disadvantage on ability checks + attack rolls in sunlight — folds into the existing Shadow / Wight / Specter sunlight-sensitivity gap as the eighth user), and Web Walker (narrative). Medusa's iconic Petrifying Gaze (Recharge 5-6, DC 13 CON in 30-ft cone, two-failure escalation Restrained → Petrified) folds into the Petrification family from batch 4.13 (Basilisk / Cockatrice / Medusa); Medusa's self-target-on-reflection mechanic is identical-shape to Basilisk's — both monsters share the gap-side mirror-vulnerability trigger. Medusa's three-attack Multiattack (two Claws + one Snake Hair OR three Poison Rays) introduces the first or-branch Multiattack option in the pack (the closest existing analog is the multiattack-with-secondary-breath swap, but Medusa's is a strict either-melee-or-ranged Multiattack rather than a swap-one-attack model). Medusa carries WIS save proficiency (the first non-Dragon non-Fiend Monstrosity with a save proficiency in the pack). Hydra Multiple Heads + Reactive Heads + regrow-heads-unless-fire-damage form the canonical hydra mechanic — composite of `Multiple Heads` (5-head head-tracker state + die-when-25-damage-or-more-on-a-turn rule + dies-when-all-heads-dead win condition + grow-2-new-heads-per-dead-head-each-turn-unless-fire-damage-this-turn regrow rule), `Reactive Heads` (extra reactions equal to heads-beyond-one for opportunity attacks only), and Multiattack-equals-head-count — three novel composite mechanics that fold into the existing head-count tracker family with a per-head-state primitive that doesn't exist today. Hydra also ships the same 6-condition-immunity profile as Death Dog from batch 4.13 (blinded / charmed / deafened / frightened / stunned / unconscious — the canonical "primitive-body" condition-immunity bundle). Hydra Hold Breath 1-hour trait is narrative. Behir Constrict (DC 18 STR save, fail = 5d8+6 bludgeoning + Grappled DC 16 + Restrained-until-grapple-ends) is the densest single-save Grappled-and-Restrained composite in the pack. Behir Swallow (DC 18 DEX save against a creature already Grappled, on fail target is swallowed; while swallowed, target has Blinded + Restrained conditions, Total Cover against outside attacks, and takes 6d6 acid at start of each Behir turn; if Behir takes 30+ damage on a single turn from swallowed creature, Behir saves DC 14 CON or regurgitates — densest swallow-cycle in the pack, joining the existing Giant Frog Swallow + Remorhaz Swallow gaps). Remorhaz's Heat Aura (5-ft emanation 3d10 fire at end of each turn) folds into the Hezrou Stench / Balor Fire Aura / Pit Fiend Fear Aura aura-trigger family — fourth user of the aura-trigger primitive after batches 4.1 + 4.2. Remorhaz's bite-then-Swallow composite is the same shape as Behir's Bite + Swallow with 5d8+5 acid + 5d8 fire damage and a 30+-damage regurgitate save, plus a "up to two creatures swallowed at a time" cap that introduces a per-statblock swallow-target-cap primitive parameterization. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on all six (Chimera 3-flavor, Drider 3-attack-any-combination, Medusa or-branch, Hydra head-count-equals-bites, Behir Bite-plus-Constrict, Remorhaz single-Bite with bonus-action Swallow); Recharge 5-6 area-save breaths on Behir + Chimera (both wireable under the slice-140 primitive but deferred for coherence as noted); poison damage riders on Drider Foreleg + Poison Burst + Medusa Snake Hair + Poison Ray (all fold into the existing poison-damage-rider gap from batch 4.13).

**Low-CR Monstrosity sweep, content-monsters-batch-4.13 (5):** Cockatrice (CR 1/2), Death Dog (CR 1), Mimic (CR 2), Basilisk (CR 3), Phase Spider (CR 3). Opens the low-CR-to-mid Monstrosity tier with five canonical adventure-staple Monstrosities below CR 4. The Monstrosity type roster moves from 12 to 17 entries (joining the existing Stirge / Ankheg / Griffon / Manticore / Owlbear / Bulette + Minotaur of Baphomet + the dinosaur cohort + the Lycanthropes). Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Cockatrice + Basilisk + Phase Spider ship `alignment: "unaligned"` (Beast-like instincts); Death Dog is NE (intelligent malice); Mimic is true-neutral (Monstrosity-flavored ambient). Pack monster total moves from 170 to 175. Cohort highlights several mechanic-level deferrals: (1) Petrification riders — Basilisk Petrifying Gaze (DC 12 CON save in 30-ft Cone, recharge 4-6, two-failure escalation: Restrained on first fail then Petrified on second; the basilisk-sees-its-reflection self-target check is a brand-new self-applied save trigger) and Cockatrice Petrifying Bite (DC 11 CON save on hit, two-failure escalation: Restrained on first then Petrified for 24 hours on second). Both fold into the two-failure-escalation save shape introduced by the Brass Sleep + Silver Paralyzing breath weapons in batches 4.5-4.8 and the slice-4.10 lycanthrope curse, parameterized with the Petrified condition. The basilisk's self-targeting on-reflection mechanic is a novel composite (the closest existing analog is the existing Vampire Forbiddance / Sunlight environmental gates, but applied as a self-vulnerability trigger to its own gaze). (2) Death Dog Bite disease (DC 12 CON save, fail = Poisoned + HP-max-no-restore-on-long-rest, repeats per 24 hours; subsequent failures decrease HP max by 1d10) — folds into the Mummy / Mummy Lord cursed-HP-max-decay-over-time family from batch 4.9 with a Poisoned-condition lock and a per-failure stacking decrement rather than a per-24-hour decrement. Death Dog also carries the broadest condition-immunity profile for a CR 1 monster in the pack (blinded / charmed / deafened / frightened / stunned / unconscious — six entries), exercising the absence of poisoned / paralyzed / petrified / exhaustion / prone — a distinctive non-Undead condition-immunity profile. (3) Mimic Adhesive trait (Object Form Only) and Shape-Shift bonus action between true blob form and object form, with the Bite + Pseudopod attacks gaining auto-grapple + Disadvantage-on-escape-checks while in object form — composite of the existing Shape-Shift gap (Vampire / Mummy Lord / Lycanthropes / Hag / Genie family) with per-form action availability + an attached-condition-with-Disadvantage-modifier-on-escape escape-modifier primitive that doesn't exist today. (4) Phase Spider Ethereal Jaunt bonus action (teleport between Material and Ethereal Planes) and Ethereal Sight trait (60-ft cross-plane vision) — first cross-plane traversal mechanic in the pack; Night Hag's Etherealness from batch 4.11 is the closest existing analog but it's a long-duration spell-cast variant rather than a bonus-action toggle. Phase Spider Bite reduce-to-0-then-Stable-Poisoned-Paralyzed shares shape with the Vampire Familiar Umbral Dagger rider from batch 4.9. (5) Web Walker narrative (consumer territory; same shape as existing Giant Spider / Wolf Spider gap). Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Death Dog + Phase Spider (Cockatrice, Mimic, Basilisk make single attacks per Attack action — three of the five Monstrosities in this batch are single-attack creatures, the densest single-batch cluster of single-attack-only Monstrosities); poison damage rider on attack (Basilisk Bite 2d6 poison + Phase Spider Bite 2d8 poison — both fold into the existing poison-damage-rider-on-attack gap with the Vrock / Hezrou / Spider cohort); recharge-4-6 area save on Basilisk Petrifying Gaze is the first non-recharge-5-6 / non-recharge-6 variant in the pack (every other Recharge action in the pack is recharge-5-6 or recharge-6), exercising the schema's `rechargeMin: 4` value for the first time outside its enum range proof; Mimic + Phase Spider Shape-Shift / Ethereal Jaunt fold into the existing Shape-Shift gap with bonus-action variants.

**Genie + Mephit cohort, content-monsters-batch-4.12 (6):** Steam Mephit (CR 1/4), Dust Mephit (CR 1/2), Ice Mephit (CR 1/2), Magma Mephit (CR 1/2), Djinni (CR 11), Efreeti (CR 11). Opens the Genie + Mephit cohorts for the Elemental type (which previously held only the four base Elementals + Invisible Stalker from batch 1.9). The Elemental roster moves from 5 to 11 entries. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. First `subtype: "genie"` and `subtype: "mephit"` users in the pack. Djinni + Efreeti both wire Magic Resistance via `{kind: "GrantMagicResistance"}` (slice-131 cohort moves from 28 to 30). Djinni + Efreeti are the first two true-neutral non-Beast statblocks in the pack alongside Weretiger from batch 4.10. The four mephits all share a tight uniform structural shape: Small, NE, walk 30 + fly 30, exhaustion + poisoned condition immunities, poison damage immunity, primordial language only; Dust + Ice + Magma additionally ship damage vulnerabilities (fire for Dust / Ice, cold for Magma — Steam Mephit is the only Mephit without a damage vulnerability). Dust + Ice + Magma + Steam ship 0.25-0.5 CR — the densest single-batch addition of low-CR Elemental content. Pack monster total moves from 164 to 170. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack absent across the entire cohort (every Mephit makes a single Claw attack per Attack action; Djinni / Efreeti have Multiattack); Death Burst on all four mephits (on-death-area-save with damage scaled per mephit type — folds into the existing Balor Death Throes gap as a low-CR mirror, the first cohort of multiple users for that primitive — Dust DC 10 DEX 2d4 bludgeoning, Ice DC 10 CON 2d4 cold, Magma DC 11 DEX 2d6 fire, Steam DC 10 DEX 2d4 fire); Mephit Recharge-6 area breaths (Dust Blinding Breath / Ice Frost Breath / Magma Fire Breath / Steam Steam Breath, all 15-ft cones — Blinding Breath alone is a non-damaging condition-on-fail variant and is the fifth user of the slice-4.5 secondary-non-damaging-breath gap; the other three carry typed damage but the engine's slice-140 breath primitive doesn't support recharge-on-6-only as a per-creature scaling parameter today — actually, the schema's `rechargeMin: 2 to 6` field supports the Recharge-6 variant via rechargeMin=6, so the Mephit damaging breaths could be wired via the slice-140 primitive; however they share their secondary-non-damaging-breath structure with the dragons' family, so the doc-track ships the entries with `traits: []` for cohesion with the existing four base Elementals); Mephit innate spellcasting envelopes (1/Day spells per mephit: Dust Sleep, Ice Fog Cloud, Magma none, Steam none — folds into the existing innate-spellcasting-envelope gap); Steam Mephit Blurred Form (Disadvantage on attacks against me unless Incapacitated — new defensive primitive that overlaps with the existing GrantDisadvantage shapes but applied to incoming attack rolls broadly rather than per-attacker, and gated on the bearer's own Incapacitated state); Djinni Create Whirlwind (concentration-based 20-ft-radius / 60-ft-high cylinder area-of-effect that moves up to 20 ft per turn, target STR DC 17 vs Restrained + 6d6 recurring thunder damage at start of turn + recurring save at end of turn to escape) — densest novel composite this batch: persistent-area-effect + concentration-binding + movement-each-turn + multi-target save-on-enter + Restrained-while-inside + recurring-damage + recurring-save-to-end. Djinni Storm Bolt's Large-or-smaller Prone-on-hit rider folds into the existing on-hit-save-or-condition gap (the closest matching shape is the Adult-Chromatic / Wereboar Charge prone rider, but applied as an attack-roll-on-hit rather than a save-or-condition save shape). Efreeti Hurl Flame (7d6 fire ranged attack) is the highest-flat-elemental-damage ranged attack in the pack for a non-Ancient-Dragon, matching the existing per-color elemental-ranged-attack riders. Djinni + Efreeti both have Spellcasting envelopes (Djinni: 5 At-Will + 3 2/Day + 5 1/Day; Efreeti: 2 At-Will + 6 1/Day), folding into the existing innate-spellcasting envelope gap. Djinni + Efreeti both carry the 30%-chance-of-Wish-spell-cast-on-behalf-of-another mechanic with 3/year usage cap and no stress to the genie (Wishes trait) — narrative / consumer territory under the wish gap. Djinni + Efreeti Elemental Restoration (1d4-day plane-respawn) is narrative analogous to Demonic / Diabolical Restoration. Mephit "Primordial (Auran / Aquan / Ignan / Terran)" subdialect specifications in the SRD language line are deferred to just "primordial" per the existing pack convention.

**Hag trio, content-monsters-batch-4.11 (3):** Sea Hag (CR 2), Green Hag (CR 3), Night Hag (CR 5). Closes the canonical SRD 5.2.1 Hag roster in a single batch. Splits across two creature types: Sea + Green ship as `Fey` (joining Blink Dog / Dryad / Satyr / Sprite from batch 1.14 — Fey roster moves from 4 to 6); Night ships as `Fiend` (joining the Demon + Devil rosters — Fiend roster grows by one to 17 entries). Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Night Hag carries cold + fire damage resistance, charmed-condition immunity, the broadest non-draconic / non-angel language list in the pack (abyssal + common + infernal + primordial), and Magic Resistance — folds into the slice-131 cohort as a new wired user (slice-131 user count moves from 27 to 28; first new MR user since Mummy Lord in batch 4.9). Sea + Green Hag both ship Amphibious (narrative; consumer territory). The three hags share four cross-cutting deferred mechanics: (1) Coven Magic (all three) — once-per-long-rest spell-cast-from-a-list (Augury / Find Familiar / Identify / Locate Object / Scrying / Unseen Servant) gated on "within 30 ft of at least two hag allies"; needs a coven-coordination predicate primitive + per-long-rest budget + spell-as-monster-action, none of which compose for a hag today, folds into the existing innate-spellcasting envelope gap with the additional ally-proximity predicate; (2) Vile Appearance (Sea Hag only) — start-of-turn aura DC 11 WIS save vs Frightened until start of target's next turn, with the 24-hour per-target immunity stamp shared shape with the Adult-Chromatic Frightful Presence / Mummy Dreadful Glare / Pit Fiend Fear Aura, restricted to Beast and Humanoid targets (a per-creature-type predicate gate the engine doesn't model today — the closest analogue is the Bite-vs-Humanoid restriction on lycanthrope curse riders); (3) Mimicry (Green Hag) — narrative animal-sound / humanoid-voice imitation with a perceive-as-imitation DC 14 WIS (Insight) check, consumer territory; (4) Death Glare (Sea Hag Recharge 5-6) — target Frightened creature within 30 ft, WIS DC 11 save fail vs instant-drop-to-0-HP-if-HP-is-20-or-less / 3d8 psychic damage otherwise; the instant-0-HP-at-or-below-threshold mechanic is the densest novel deferral in this batch (composite of a target-condition-predicate `frightened` + an HP-threshold-check + a binary-outcome resolution branching on HP — closest existing analog is Sea Hag's own Vile Appearance's per-target-immunity stamp, but the HP-threshold predicate is genuinely new). Night Hag-specific deferrals: Soul Bag — a per-statblock attached-stateful-item-as-entity with AC 15 / HP 20 / resistance-to-all-damage + 7-day-recreation-after-destruction lifecycle (extends the Erinyes Magic Rope gap from batch 4.2 with additional HP / resistance / recreation parameters and a "while-holding-bag" trigger predicate gating an entire action like Nightmare Haunting); Nightmare Haunting (1/Day, requires Soul Bag) — Dream-spell-as-monster-action with on-Ethereal-Plane gating, a creature-Hit-Point-maximum-decrease-on-Dream-damage rider, a soul-trap-on-kill rider, and a no-raise-from-dead-until-soul-released ghost-state rider — composite of spell-as-monster-action + cross-plane gating + multiple novel kill-state riders, the densest novel deferral surfaced this batch; Etherealness at-will spell, Phantasmal Killer 2/Day, Plane Shift 2/Day (self-only) and Magic Missile L4 at-will all fold into the innate-spellcasting envelope gap; Shape-Shift bonus action (Small or Medium Humanoid form, same stats other than size) folds into the Vampire / lycanthrope Shape-Shift gap. Green Hag-specific deferrals: Spellcasting envelope (Dancing Lights + Disguise Self + Invisibility + Minor Illusion + Ray of Sickness L3 at-will, all using WIS as spellcasting ability — first Hag innate-spellcasting list with non-INT spellcasting ability, exercising the spell-ability-key parameterization of the existing innate-spellcasting envelope); Disguise Self with a 24-hour duration (vs RAW base of 1 hour) and Invisibility with a "leaves no tracks" qualifier are two narrow parameterizations of existing spells. All three hags share the on-hit-Poison damage rider on Claw shape: Green Hag's Claw adds 1d6 poison damage on hit (folds into the existing on-hit-poison-damage-rider gap shared with Giant Spider / Wolf Spider / Ankheg / Bone Devil / Assassin / Vrock / Hezrou); Sea + Night Hag Claws have no rider, exercising the absence-of-rider case. Pack monster total moves from 161 to 164. Fey type roster moves from 4 to 6 (Sea + Green Hag); Fiend type roster moves from 16 to 17 (Night Hag).

**Lycanthrope cohort, content-monsters-batch-4.10 (5):** Wererat (CR 2), Werewolf (CR 3), Wereboar (CR 4), Weretiger (CR 4), Werebear (CR 5). Closes the canonical SRD 5.2.1 Lycanthrope roster in a single batch (every SRD 5.2.1 lycanthrope now ships) and adds the first explicit `subtype: "lycanthrope"` cohort to the pack. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. The cohort opens a tight alignment span: NG (Werebear), NE (Wereboar), LE (Wererat), CE (Werewolf), N (Weretiger) — Werebear is the first NG monster in the pack and Weretiger the first true-neutral entry that isn't an unaligned beast. None of the five carry savingThrows (all six abilities at flat modifier, no proficiency). Wererat + Werewolf + Weretiger + Werebear ship `darkvision: 60`; Wereboar is the only lycanthrope without darkvision. Pack monster total moves from 156 to 161. Note on form-specific stats: the SRD entries specify form-specific speed and action availability (e.g. Werebear: "Speed 30 ft., 40 ft. (bear form only), Climb 30 ft. (bear form only)"; Wereboar: "30 ft., 40 ft. (boar form only)"). The pack ships true-form speeds only (the schema is a single statblock per entry, no form variants); form-specific bonuses (Werebear's bear-form 40-walk + climb 30, Wereboar / Weretiger / Werewolf's animal-form 40-walk) are deferred under the existing Vampire-style Shape-Shift gap. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on all five (with the "multiattack-with-options" pattern — every lycanthrope makes two of one weapon attack with a one-attack Bite/Gore swap-in, the same shape exercised by the Metallic Dragon Multiattack-with-secondary-breath gap); Shape-Shift bonus action across all five (folds into the Vampire Shape-Shift gap with a per-tier-statblock-name swap — Werebear true/hybrid/bear, Wereboar true/hybrid/boar etc — and a per-form action availability restriction shared with Vampire's "Vampire Form Only" / "Bat or Vampire Form Only" labels on Multiattack + Grave Strike + Bite); Lycanthropy curse rider on Bite (Werebear) / Gore (Wereboar) / Bite (Wererat) / Bite (Weretiger) / Bite (Werewolf) — every lycanthrope's signature attack carries a CON save (DC 11-14 per CR tier) vs cursed-on-drop-to-0-turn-into-the-same-lycanthrope-under-GM-control with a 24-hour per-target immunity stamp on save success. This is the densest single primitive deferral surfacing in this batch: composite of on-hit-save-or-condition + on-drop-to-0-spawn-specific-statblock-with-set-HP + the per-target 24-hour immunity stamp (shared shape with Mummy Dreadful Glare + Adult Chromatic Frightful Presence) + the GM-control variant of the existing summon-spawn primitive family. The five distinct DCs (DC 11 / 12 / 12 / 13 / 14 for Wererat / Wereboar / Werewolf / Weretiger / Werebear) exercise the per-tier DC scaling first introduced by the Chromatic / Metallic dragon breath weapons. Wereboar Tusk Charge (movement-conditional 2d6 extra damage + Prone if moved 20+ feet straight before hit) folds into the existing Charge gap (Boar / Minotaur / Unicorn / Allosaurus / Triceratops / Mammoth). Werewolf Pack Tactics (advantage on attack rolls when an ally is within 5 feet of target) joins the existing Pack Tactics gap (Tough / Warrior Infantry / Giant Rat / Dire Wolf — five users now). Weretiger Prowl bonus action (move up to speed without provoking Opportunity Attacks + Hide at end of movement) is a novel mechanic-level deferral: composite of an opportunity-attack-immunity-for-this-movement primitive (similar in shape to the Pteranodon Flyby gap but covering all directions rather than only flight-away) plus an inline Hide-action chain. Werebear / Wereboar / Wererat / Weretiger / Werewolf all carry typed weapon Gear (4 Handaxes / 6 Javelins / Hand Crossbow / Longbow / Longbow) referenced by their Multiattack actions, exercising the existing pack convention of associating weapon-Gear with the monster's Multiattack chain rather than carrying typed item-instances per statblock. The five animal forms (bear / boar / rat / tiger / wolf) all already ship in the pack as standalone Beast statblocks (Brown Bear, Boar, Giant Rat, Mastiff-as-proxy, Wolf) — when monster Shape-Shift wires, the lycanthrope-form-into-existing-Beast-statblock route is the cleanest install path, avoiding a per-lycanthrope form duplicate.

**Vampire + mummy roster, content-monsters-batch-4.9 (5):** Mummy (CR 3), Vampire Familiar (CR 3), Vampire Spawn (CR 5), Vampire (CR 13), Mummy Lord (CR 15). First broad Undead expansion since the original seed; the Undead roster moves from 8 entries (Skeleton, Zombie, Shadow, Ghoul, Specter, Wight, Ghost, Wraith) to 13. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage R/I/V / condition immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. The cohort exercises every existing structural-gap shape simultaneously: damage **vulnerabilities** on Mummy + Mummy Lord (fire — the seventh and eighth pack monsters with `damageVulnerabilities` populated, joining Skeleton bludgeoning + Earth Elemental thunder + Animated Rug of Smothering slashing + Awakened Shrub / Awakened Tree / Treant fire); broad condition immunities on Mummy + Mummy Lord (charmed + exhaustion + frightened + paralyzed + poisoned — the densest condition-immunity profile in the pack for Undead, matching the canonical Undead "type immunities" baseline RAW grants by creature type); necrotic resistance on all three Vampire variants. Mummy Lord ships Magic Resistance via `{kind: "GrantMagicResistance"}` (slice-131 cohort moves from 26 to 27 — the first new MR user since batch 4.2). Vampire + Mummy Lord both ship Legendary Resistance 3/Day, adding two new users to the existing gap (twelve 3/Day users in the pack now after Aboleth + 5 Adult Chromatics + 5 Adult Metallics + Balor + Mummy Lord + Vampire). Pack monster total moves from 151 to 156. Defers under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on all five (Mummy / Mummy Lord / Vampire / Vampire Spawn / Vampire Familiar — every entry except Vampire Familiar combines a melee attack chain with a special ability, the densest single-batch addition to the existing Multiattack list); on-hit composite riders that fold into multiple gap entries — Mummy + Mummy Lord Rotting Fist (necrotic damage rider + curse + "can't regain HP" + HP-max-decay-over-time + reduce-to-0-turns-to-dust composite — the densest single-attack composite in the pack, folding into the on-hit save-or-condition gap + the Wraith / Wight / Bearded Devil wound-no-heal family + a brand new HP-max-decay-over-time primitive that doesn't exist today); Vampire + Vampire Spawn Bite (CON save vs necrotic damage + HP-max-reduction-on-fail + caster-self-heal-on-fail — composite of the Wraith Life Drain max-HP-reduction gap + a Bite-vs-charmed/grappled/restrained/willing-target restriction predicate and the Vampire's "buried target becomes Vampire Spawn after sunset" on-kill-spawn rider, folding into the Wraith Create Specter / Shadow Spawn gap); Vampire Spawn + Vampire Claw + Grave Strike auto-grapple (on-hit-auto-grapple gap, shared with Constrictor Snake / Ankheg / Couatl / Marilith); Vampire + Vampire Spawn Charm (Recharge 5-6) as a Charm-Person-spell-as-monster-action with 24-hour duration and the auto-willing-bite mechanic — folds into the spell-as-monster-action gap with an additional condition-rider state (`willing recipient of vampire's bite`) the engine doesn't model; Vampire Familiar Umbral Dagger's reduce-to-0-then-stable-poisoned-paralyzed rider is a novel mechanic-level deferral (the reduce-to-0 + auto-Stable + auto-poisoned + Paralyzed-while-Poisoned-chain shape doesn't fit any existing gap, fold composes the existing condition stack with a new on-reduce-to-0 trigger and an instant-Stable outcome that the death-save machinery doesn't currently expose). Mummy + Mummy Lord Dreadful Glare (single-target WIS save vs Frightened with 24-hour per-target immunity stamp on success — same shape as the Adult-Chromatic / Pit-Fiend Frightful Presence aura, only single-target rather than aura); Mummy Lord Spellcasting (full innate cleric envelope: At Will Dispel Magic / Thaumaturgy, 1/Day Animate Dead / Harm / Insect Plague L7 — folds into the innate-spellcasting envelope gap with the per-day variant); Mummy Lord Whirlwind of Sand reaction (AC +2 + 60-ft teleport + blinded-condition area-rider on creatures within 5 ft of destination — composes the monster-reaction gap + monster-teleport-as-action gap + multi-target condition rider); Mummy Lord Legendary Actions (Dread Command 2nd-level Command spell + Glare repeat + Necrotic Strike — folds into the existing Legendary Actions gap); Mummy Lord Undead Restoration (24-hour respawn-from-intact-heart with the heart as an AC 17 / HP 10 / fire-only-damage object that lives in the lair — narrative, consumer territory). Vampire Misty Escape (on-drop-to-0 auto-Shape-Shift to mist, must reach resting place in 2 hours, Paralyzed-until-1-HP-regained on return — composite of on-drop-to-0 trigger + auto-action-substitution + a 1-hour duration counter + a forced-state-on-recovery rider — composite of multiple deferred shapes), Vampire Spider Climb (narrative; consumer territory, joins existing pack note), Vampire Weakness (Forbiddance / Running Water / Stake to the Heart / Sunlight: all four are environmental / situational riders — Running Water and Sunlight ship "20 damage if-you-end/start-turn-in" recurring environmental damage variants, similar shape to the existing environmental-conditional gap but specific to the Undead Vampire weakness family; Stake to the Heart is the destroyed-if-piercing-while-incapacitated kill rider; Forbiddance is narrative residence-entry restriction). Vampire Shape-Shift (transform between Vampire / Tiny bat / Medium cloud of mist forms with per-form modified ability scores + a Vampire-form-only restriction on Multiattack and Grave Strike — folds into the existing Shapechanger gap with a third-form variant that's a status / movement primitive rather than a creature transform). Vampire's "Multiattack (Vampire Form Only)" + "Grave Strike (Vampire Form Only)" + "Bite (Bat or Vampire Form Only)" introduce the first per-form-restricted-action shape in the pack (similar in spirit to the polymorph gap but applying to monster-action availability rather than active-form-statblock substitution). The Vampire Familiar's `conditionImmunities: ["charmed"]` carries an unmodeled qualifier (RAW: "Charmed except from its vampire master"); the engine has no qualifier system for condition-immunity exceptions, so the pack ships the broader form with the qualifier noted as a deferral, mirroring the existing slice-112 nonmagical-B/P/S qualifier treatment. Vampire Familiar's Vampiric Connection trait (telepathic communication with its master while on same plane + master can perceive through familiar's senses) is narrative cross-creature linking, deferred under the existing Shield Guardian / amulet-bound cross-entity reference gap.

**Ancient Metallic Dragon ladder, content-monsters-batch-4.8 (5):** Ancient Brass Dragon (CR 20), Ancient Copper Dragon (CR 21), Ancient Bronze Dragon (CR 22), Ancient Silver Dragon (CR 23), Ancient Gold Dragon (CR 24). Closes the Metallic Dragon ladder and completes the full dragon-by-age-tier coverage in the pack: both Chromatic and Metallic ladders now ship at all four age tiers (Wyrmling + Young + Adult + Ancient × 10 colors = 40 statblocks, fully matching SRD 5.2.1's printed dragon roster). Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB; non-lair stats only (lair-version HP, LR uses, and breath-DC bumps dropped per the single-statblock-variant constraint, same as Ancient Chromatics in batch 4.4). Each ships a `breathWeapon` field consumed by the slice-140 primitive (wired-breath-weapon cohort moves from 37 to 42 — every dragon Adult and Ancient tier statblock now has a wired breath). Gargantuan size across the cohort; CR 20 to 24 mirrors the Ancient Chromatic ladder exactly (Ancient Brass at CR 20 ties with Ancient White as the lowest-CR Ancient; Ancient Gold at CR 24 ties with Ancient Red as the highest-CR statblock in the pack). PB +6 on Ancient Brass alone (matching Ancient White); PB +7 on Ancient Copper / Bronze / Silver / Gold (the second cohort of PB +7 users after the Ancient Chromatics, exercising the same upper-end of the schema's PB range cap of 9). Senses: blindsight 60 + darkvision 120 across the cohort (identical to the Ancient Chromatic tier). Each Ancient Metallic carries its canonical elemental immunity (fire / acid / lightning / cold / fire); Ancient Bronze + Gold ship Amphibious as narrative. Breath geometry mirrors the Ancient Chromatic split for color: Brass / Copper / Bronze line breaths (90 / 90 / 120 ft), Silver / Gold cone breaths (90 ft each). DCs scale 21 / 22 / 23 / 24 / 24; damage dice expand: 13d8 fire / 14d8 acid / 15d10 lightning / 15d8 cold / 13d10 fire. Ancient Bronze's 120-ft line breath ties with Ancient Blue's as the widest line breath in the pack. Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on all five (with the doubled "multiattack-with-options" sub-shape — one Rend can be replaced by either a secondary breath use or a Spellcasting use, same shape as the Adult Metallic tier); Legendary Resistance 4/Day on all five (folds into the existing gap alongside the Ancient Chromatics + Pit Fiend at the 4/Day tier — eleven 4/Day users in the pack now); per-color Legendary Action menus (Pounce + a per-color signature; Brass Blazing Light + Scorching Sands area-save, Bronze Guiding Light + Thunderclap area-save, Copper Giggling Magic 1d8 + Mind Jolt, Silver Chill + Cold Gale push, Gold Banish + Guiding Light — same composite shapes as the Adult Metallic tier with damage and DC scaled up; Copper Giggling Magic's d8 debuff variant scales the per-CR-tier numeric exercise of the d6 / d8 / dN family); innate Spellcasting on all five (each carries an at-will + 1/Day-each spell list including the canonical Shapechange at-will entry, with the spell levels and DCs scaled to PB +7); secondary non-damaging breath weapons (Sleep / Slowing / Repulsion / Paralyzing / Weakening, with Ancient-tier DCs and scaled-up rider parameters — Brass Sleep Breath jumps from a 60-ft cone at Adult to 90-ft cone at Ancient, with 10-minute unconscious; Bronze Repulsion Breath retains the 60-ft push from Adult tier, the same forced-movement gap user; Silver Paralyzing Breath retains the consecutive-failure escalation shape; Gold Weakening Breath introduces a 1d10 damage-roll-subtract — the largest die in the per-tier scaling, completing the family numeric exercise: 1d4 at Wyrmling, 1d6 at Young + Adult, 1d10 at Ancient). On-hit elemental damage rider on Rend ships at Ancient tier with 2d6 / 2d8 elemental damage on top of slashing (the Adult Metallic Rend ships with 1d8; the Ancient tier doubles the rider — the same per-tier scaling exercised by the Adult-to-Ancient Chromatic Rend riders). Brand-new mechanic-level deferral: Ancient Brass Scorching Sands legendary action (DEX DC 20 vs 8d8 fire + speed-halved-until-end-of-target's-next-turn) introduces a single-target speed-halved-for-one-turn rider that overlaps with the Adult Copper Slowing Breath area-save shape but applied as a single-target on-fail damage rider — the slowing half is the same gap, the per-target single-cast variant is a small parameterization addition. Both 4/Day Legendary Resistance and full Legendary Actions menus on every Ancient Metallic round out the existing gap with the same composite shapes as the Ancient Chromatic cohort, just parameterized differently. Pack monster total moves from 146 to 151; the wired-breath-weapon cohort grows from 37 to 42.

**Metallic Wyrmling ladder, content-monsters-batch-4.7 (5):** Brass Dragon Wyrmling (CR 1), Copper Dragon Wyrmling (CR 1), Bronze Dragon Wyrmling (CR 2), Silver Dragon Wyrmling (CR 2), Gold Dragon Wyrmling (CR 3). Opens the Metallic Wyrmling tier below the existing Young + Adult Metallic ladder, mirroring slice 4.3 (Chromatic Wyrmlings) for the Metallic side. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Each ships a `breathWeapon` field consumed by the slice-140 primitive (wired-breath-weapon cohort moves from 32 to 37 — every dragon Wyrmling now has a wired breath). Brass + Copper share the new CR 1 floor for the Dragon type (the previous floor was Black / Green / White Wyrmling at CR 2), making them the two lowest-CR Wyrmlings and the only Dragons in the pack below CR 2. CR span 1 to 3 mirrors the Chromatic Wyrmling tier (CR 2 to 4) one CR step lower across the cohort. Breath geometry mirrors the Chromatic per-color split: Brass / Copper / Bronze line breaths (20 / 20 / 40 ft), Silver / Gold cone breaths (15 ft each). DCs scale 11 / 11 / 12 / 13 / 13; damage dice 4d6 fire / 4d8 acid / 3d10 lightning / 4d8 cold / 4d10 fire. Each Wyrmling carries its canonical elemental immunity (fire / acid / lightning / cold / fire). Silver Wyrmling's Rend deals **piercing** damage (every other Metallic Wyrmling's Rend deals slashing — the only Metallic Wyrmling whose primary attack is piercing rather than slashing; the higher Silver tiers revert to slashing). Bronze + Gold Wyrmlings ship Amphibious (narrative; consumer territory). All five ship `traits: []` (breath weapon lives on the dedicated field). Brass + Copper Wyrmlings lack Multiattack in RAW (a single Rend per Attack action, the only Multiattack-less Wyrmlings in the pack — every other Wyrmling, Chromatic or Metallic, makes two Rends per Attack); Bronze, Silver, Gold Wyrmlings have the standard two-Rend Multiattack. All five also carry a *secondary non-damaging breath* that folds into the slice-4.5 secondary-non-damaging-breath gap family (Brass Sleep, Bronze Repulsion, Copper Slowing, Gold Weakening, Silver Paralyzing) — same per-color signature as the Young / Adult tiers, with the Wyrmling DCs scaled down (DC 11 to DC 13). Bronze Wyrmling's Repulsion Breath uses the same 30-ft cone shape with a 30-ft straight push and Prone condition; the push distance is halved from the Adult tier (60 ft) but otherwise identical to the Young tier (30 ft straight + Prone), exercising the same forced-movement primitive gap. Silver Wyrmling's Paralyzing Breath introduces the consecutive-failures escalation shape (incapacitated then paralyzed) — same shape as the Young Silver Paralyzing Breath at one CR higher, identical mechanic with DCs scaled down. Gold Wyrmling's Weakening Breath uses a 15-ft cone (Young Gold's was 30-ft cone, Adult Gold's 60-ft cone) — same recurring-save Disadvantage-on-STR-D20-tests + 1d4 damage-roll-subtract rider (1d4 in the Wyrmling tier, 1d6 in Young + Adult — the per-tier scaling of the damage-roll-subtract die is the first numeric scale exercised in this gap family). Deferred under existing engine gaps: Multiattack on Bronze + Silver + Gold (Brass + Copper Wyrmlings have no Multiattack — narrative absence); Amphibious narrative on Bronze + Gold; Metallic Rend exercises the absence-of-elemental-damage-rider case (no elemental rider at Wyrmling tier, same as the Young Metallic tier — the elemental rider first appears at the Adult Metallic tier). Pack monster total moves from 141 to 146; the wired-breath-weapon cohort grows from 32 to 37.

**Adult Metallic Dragon tier-up, content-monsters-batch-4.6 (5):** Adult Brass Dragon (CR 13), Adult Copper Dragon (CR 14), Adult Bronze Dragon (CR 15), Adult Silver Dragon (CR 16), Adult Gold Dragon (CR 17). Mirror of slice 1.18 (Adult Chromatics) for the Metallic ladder. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB; non-lair stats only (lair-version HP, LR uses, and breath-DC bumps dropped per the single-statblock-variant constraint). Each ships a `breathWeapon` field consumed by the slice-140 primitive (wired-breath-weapon cohort moves from 27 to 32). Huge size; CR 13 to 17 (Adult Gold at CR 17 ties with Adult Red as the second-highest-CR Adult-tier statblock in the pack, behind only the Ancient Chromatic and Pit Fiend tier). PB +5 on Brass / Copper / Bronze / Silver; PB +6 on Gold (the only Adult Metallic at the higher PB tier, matching Adult Red). Each carries its canonical elemental immunity (fire for Brass + Gold, acid for Copper, lightning for Bronze, cold for Silver); Adult Bronze + Gold ship Amphibious as narrative. Breath geometry expands from the Young tier: Brass / Copper line breaths grow from 40 to 60 ft, Bronze line breath grows from 60 to 90 ft, Silver / Gold cone breaths grow from 30 to 60 ft. DCs scale 18 / 18 / 19 / 20 / 21; damage dice expand: 10d8 fire / 12d8 acid / 10d10 lightning / 12d8 cold / 12d10 fire. The cohort exercises every existing dragon-tier mechanic at once: Legendary Resistance 3/Day on all five (folds into the existing gap alongside Adult Chromatics + Aboleth), full Legendary Action menus (3 uses/round, drawing from Pounce + a per-color signature action — Brass Blazing Light / Bronze Guiding Light + Thunderclap area-save / Copper Giggling Magic d6-debuff + Mind Jolt / Silver Chill + Cold Gale area-save / Gold Banish + Guiding Light — folding into the existing Adult-Chromatic legendary-actions gap with two novel sub-mechanics: Bronze Thunderclap's "deafened until end of next turn" rider on a thunder-damage area save and Silver Cold Gale's combined damage + 30-ft forced push extends the Balor pull-and-prone gap further), innate Spellcasting on all five (each Adult Metallic carries an at-will + 1/Day-each spell list including a uniquely-Metallic Shapechange-into-beast-or-humanoid at-will entry that overlaps with the existing polymorph planner gap but with the additional flat-no-temp-HP / no-concentration qualifiers), and a secondary non-damaging breath on all five (Sleep / Slowing / Repulsion / Paralyzing / Weakening, scaled-up DCs from the Young tier) folds into the slice-4.5 secondary-non-damaging-breath gap family. The Multiattack on each Adult Metallic exercises a more elaborate "multiattack-with-options" sub-shape than the Young tier: each can replace one Rend with either a secondary-breath use or a Spellcasting use, doubling the option count. On-hit elemental damage rider on Rend ships at Adult tier (1d8 elemental damage on top of slashing for every Adult Metallic, in contrast to the Young Metallic's pure-slashing Rend), exercising the same on-hit-elemental-rider primitive family as the Chromatic Rends across all four tiers. Adult Copper Giggling Magic's 1d6 subtract-from-D20-test debuff is the first non-flat-modifier per-attack-roll-modifier in the pack (closest existing is Bardic Inspiration adding a die, but Giggling Magic subtracts a die — same primitive shape, opposite sign). Adult Gold Banish (Charisma save vs 3d6 force damage + Incapacitated + transported to demiplane until start of attacker's next turn, then returned) is a brand-new legendary-action shape composing the existing-condition (Incapacitated) primitive with a temporary-removal-from-encounter primitive that doesn't exist; folds into the existing Legendary Actions gap as a novel composite.

**Young Metallic Dragon opener, content-monsters-batch-4.5 (5):** Young Brass Dragon (CR 6), Young Copper Dragon (CR 7), Young Bronze Dragon (CR 8), Young Silver Dragon (CR 9), Young Gold Dragon (CR 10). Opens the Metallic Dragon ladder with the canonical Young tier, mirroring slice 1.17 (Young Chromatics) and giving the pack its first non-Chromatic dragons. Every entry sourced verbatim from `references/srd-markdown/monsters-A-Z.md` on AC / HP / abilities / saves / damage immunities / senses / CR / XP / PB. Each ships a `breathWeapon` field consumed by the slice-140 primitive (wired-breath-weapon cohort moves from 22 to 27). The cohort exercises the new "metallic alignment block" — three Lawful Good (Bronze, Silver, Gold) versus two Chaotic Good (Brass, Copper), the first cluster of Good-aligned Dragons in the pack (every prior dragon was Chaotic or Lawful Evil). Breath geometry mirrors the Chromatics with a different per-color mapping: Brass / Copper / Bronze carry line breaths (40 / 40 / 60 ft), Silver / Gold cone breaths (30 ft each). DCs scale 14 / 14 / 15 / 17 / 17; damage dice 11d6 fire / 9d8 acid / 9d10 lightning / 11d8 cold / 10d10 fire.
