Other planners that emit `ConditionApplied` (movement, weapon-mastery, contested, sacred-weapon, stunning-strike, frenzy, the reactive-spells branch) don't yet gate — none of them currently apply Frightened or any other condition the engine actually carries an immunity for, so the RAW impact is zero today. As new immunity-relevant conditions come online (Charmed, Paralyzed, Poisoned, Stunned interactions), wire the helper in those planners on demand. |
| **~~On-hit trigger system~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 7 wired across attacker- and target-side (slice 61 attacker-side: divine-favor, searing-smite, wrathful-smite, thunderous-smite, branding-smite, plus Crusader's Mantle in slice 63; slice 88 target-side: hex + bestow-curse's extra-damage variant); 5 still deferred (ensnaring-strike, hail-of-thorns, blinding-smite, lightning-arrow, ray-of-enfeeblement) | Slice 61 added the `consumeOnTrigger` flag on `OnEvent` effects (one-shot riders lift their parent condition after firing) plus the simple AddDamage attacker-side rider used by the smite cohort. Slice 88 threaded `AppliedCondition` provenance through `dispatchTriggers` and added the `event.attackerIsSource` fact, which lets a target-side rider filter on "the creature attacking me is this curse's caster." `findAppliedConditionForOnEvent` walks `character.appliedConditions` to map an `OnEvent.id` back to the applied condition that contributed it, and the source's `sourceCharacterId` flows into facts. Both spell planners (buff + save) now stamp `intent.characterId` as `sourceCharacterId` on `ConditionApplied` events so the source link is always populated for spell-applied conditions. Remaining deferrals need separate primitives: save-or-restrain rider for Ensnaring Strike, AoE-on-hit for Hail of Thorns and Lightning Arrow, condition-on-hit for Blinding Smite, on-attack-output debuff for Ray of Enfeeblement. |
| **~~On-miss trigger primitive~~** ✓ shipped | 1 wired (Fighter L13 Studied Attacks). | Slice 108 added the `event.targetIsSource` fact in dispatch (mirror of `event.attackerIsSource`) and a `sourceFromEventTarget?: boolean` flag on `ApplyConditionToAttacker`. The on-miss filter itself (`event.hit === false`) was already supported via the existing fact, but Studied Attacks needed a per-target tracker — when `sourceFromEventTarget` is true, the dispatcher stamps `sourceCharacterId = event.targetId` on the emitted ConditionApplied so SetAdvantageVsSource on the applied condition keys against the missed creature. The `studied-target-active` condition pairs `SetAdvantageVsSource(on:'attack', advantage)` with a consume-on-next-attack OnEvent rider (`attackerIsSelf && targetIsSource`, consumeOnTrigger) that lifts the condition after the fighter's next attack against the studied creature. Known limitations: (1) RAW "before end of your next turn" time-window expiry isn't modeled. (2) Consecutive misses against the same target don't refresh because ConditionApplied dedupes by conditionId while the consume rider still fires. Both are documented on the `studied-target-active` condition. |
| **~~Composite-buff condition~~** ✓ shipped (content) | 3 wired (haste, blur, pass-without-trace) | Slice 73 confirmed the "composite-buff" gap was a content-authoring gap, not an engine gap: conditions already support multiple effects in their `effects` array. Haste ships as a condition with four sibling effects (`ModifySpeed multiply 2`, `AddModifier ac +2`, `SetAdvantage save:DEX advantage`, `ModifyActionEconomy extraAction +1`). Blur uses `ImposeDisadvantageOnAttackers`. Pass without Trace uses `AddModifier { skill: 'stealth' } +10` and is applied to caster + allies via the existing buff mechanic (consumer lists allies in cast intent). Mirror Image's duplicate-pool wired in slice 124 (see Attack-roll-buff row). Remaining: beacon-of-hope (needs death-save-advantage primitive + heal-maximize). |
| **~~Caster-chosen options at cast time~~** ✓ shipped | 8 wired (chromatic-orb, enlarge-reduce, calm-emotions, command, enhance-ability, bestow-curse, spirit-shroud, elemental-weapon). Every PHB 2024 spell with a caster-chosen option at cast time now ships wired. Slice 90 added the item-buff damage-type extension (`extraDamageDice` + `extraDamageType` on `ItemTemporaryBuff` + `ItemBuffAppliedEvent`) and the dedicated `engine.plan.elementalWeapon` planner; the attack planner rolls the extra dice on hit (doubled on crit) and adds a second damage component of the chosen type to mitigation. | Slice 82 introduced the `CasterChoice` discriminated-union on `CastSpellIntent` plus `casterChoosesDamageType: { allowed: DamageType[] }` on attack mechanics. Slice 83 added the `'variant'` discriminator case (`{ kind: 'variant', value: string }`) plus `casterChoosesVariant: { variants: [{ key, conditionId }] }` on buff mechanics. Slice 84 ported the same `casterChoosesVariant` shape to save mechanics — the variant key picks the condition that applies on a failed save. The buff and save resolvers share a `resolveVariantConditionId` helper. Slices 85 (Command, 5-variant save), 86 (Enhance Ability, 6-variant buff), and 87 (Bestow Curse, 4-variant save) ship as pure data on top of the primitives. Bestow Curse's four conditions were narrative-only at slice-87 ship time; slice 88 wired the extra-damage variant via the target-side source-filtered rider, slice 92 wired the inactive-turn variant via the `recurringSave` condition field, and slice 96 wired the attack-disadvantage variant via the new `SetAdvantageVsSource` effect. The remaining variant (nested ability sub-choice) still needs its own primitive. Same planner validation pattern throughout: throws on missing / wrong-kind / unknown-key choices. Distinct from the `PendingChoice` protocol, which models deferred decisions persisted in state (level-up choices). |
| **~~Reaction system~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 5 wired across slices (counterspell, shield, absorb-elements, sanctuary, plus feather-fall via passive-effect side door). Future spells like Silvery Barbs (reroll a d20 from a different creature) will reuse the same dedicated-reaction-planner pattern. | The engine doesn't have a generic `ReactionRegistered` event + `apply`-side reaction window. Instead each reaction spell ships as a dedicated planner the consumer calls before/after the triggering event: planShield (after AttackRolled), planCounterspell (after a SpellCastDeclared from another caster), planConsumeGuidance (when the bearer wants to spend their d4), planAbsorbElements (after a DamageApplied of a matching element), and planSanctuaryWardSave (before an attack against a sanctuary-warded creature, slice 107). AbsorbElements specifically uses an event-sourcing-friendly approach: rather than mutate the triggering DamageApplied, it emits a compensating Healed event for the absorbed half — and the per-type `absorb-elements-charged-X-active` condition (acid / cold / fire / lightning / thunder) carries the on-next-hit rider via `OnEvent + AddDamage + consumeOnTrigger`. Slot-level scaling on the rider (RAW: +1d6 per slot above 1st) isn't modeled — the dice are hardcoded at 1d6. Sanctuary takes the inverse direction: the attacker rolls a WIS save against the caster's spell DC; on failure a `SanctuaryProtected` event records the outcome and the consumer drops the attack. The "spell ends if bearer attacks" RAW clause rides on an OnEvent rider with consumeOnTrigger on the `sanctuary-active` condition (AttackRolled with attackerIsSelf); the "harmful spell / deals damage" clauses are not modeled (no SpellCast-with-hostile-target or dealtDamage facts). Feather Fall slipped this bucket entirely via slice 81's passive `GrantFallingProtection` on `planFalling`. |
| **~~Movement-mode condition~~** ✓ shipped | 2 wired (fly, spider-climb). Levitate still deferred — RAW is a vertical-only positional effect, not a movement-mode addition. | `ModifySpeed` effect kind already supports `mode: 'fly' \| 'climb'`. Fly + Spider Climb wire as buff conditions carrying ModifySpeed entries. Slice 77 retrofit `getEffectiveSpeed` so ModifySpeed entries actually affect the engine's move planner — also retrofits Fast Movement, Unarmored Movement, Roving, Haste, and the Grappled/Restrained/Paralyzed/Petrified/Unconscious zero-speed conditions (which all already carried the appropriate ModifySpeed entries in the pack but were ignored by the planner). |
| **Transformation handler** (spell variant) | ~2 (alter-self, gaseous-form) | Spell-side transformation; piggybacks on the existing `wildShape` / `polymorph` pattern but with spell-defined target shapes. |
| **~~AC-buff condition~~** ✓ shipped | 2 wired (shield-of-faith, barkskin) | Shield of Faith is the simple case — a condition with `AddModifier target:'ac' value:2`, which already worked via existing primitives once authored. Barkskin needs floor semantics (AC bumps to 17 if natural is lower, regardless of armor). Slice 74 adds a `SetACFloor` Effect kind, an `acFloors` collector on EffectAccumulator, and a floor check in `computeAC` that bumps the natural total and stamps a `floor:<source>` breakdown entry. Distinct from OverrideACFormula (which replaces the formula entirely and only applies unarmored). |
| **~~Temp-HP grant primitive~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 1 wired (false-life). Heroism still deferred — needs a recurring-rider primitive for "start-of-turn temp HP." Aid was a misclassification — its 5-per-target buff writes to `hp.maxBonus`, not temp HP, and already wires via the existing `aid-buffed` condition. | Slice 75 adds a `temp-hp` SpellMechanic kind plus a planner that rolls `amountDice + flatAmount + extraPerSlotLevel * (slotLevel - spellLevel)` per target and emits `TempHPGranted`. The existing `applyTempHPGranted` reducer already implements RAW max-not-additive semantics. False Life ships with `1d4 + 4 + 5/slot`. |
| **~~Recurring-rider primitive~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 1 wired (heroism). Aura of Vitality (heal-per-turn), Phantasmal Force (per-turn psychic), and Hex (recurring on-attack damage) still deferred — Hex needs the on-hit cohort-with-target-side-condition path; Aura of Vitality and Phantasmal Force just need authoring once we add `bard` / `wizard` casters with damage variants. | Slice 79 adds a `recurring` SpellMechanic kind (effect: 'temp-hp' \| 'heal' \| 'damage', optional amountDice / flatAmount / addCasterAbilityMod / damageType). New `engine.plan.tickRecurring({ casterId, targetId })` planner that the consumer calls at the start of each target's turn while concentration holds. Heroism wires the spell's two-part shape: a `buff` mechanic applies `heroic-active` (Frightened immunity via GrantConditionImmunity) at cast, and the `recurring` mechanic emits TempHPGranted equal to the caster's CHA modifier per tick. |
| **~~Item-buff condition~~** ✓ shipped | 2 wired (magic-weapon, elemental-weapon). Holy Weapon is wired separately as a self-buff condition (slice 73) since its bonus applies to "your weapon attacks" generically, not a specific instance. | Slice 76 added `ItemInstance.temporaryBuff` (attackBonus, damageBonus, sourceEffectInstanceId, source) plus `ItemBuffApplied` / `ItemBuffRemoved` events and reducers, with `engine.plan.magicWeapon` driving the cast (slot consume, concentration start, buff stamp). Slice 90 extended the shape with `extraDamageDice` + `extraDamageType` for Elemental Weapon's per-hit elemental rider; the attack planner rolls the extra dice on hit (doubled on crit) and emits a second damage component of the chosen type, and `engine.plan.elementalWeapon` drives the cast with slot-tier scaling (+1/1d4 → +2/2d4 → +3/3d4 at slots 3-4 / 5-6 / 7+). `clearConcentrationEffect` walks item instances and strips any buff tagged with the dropped effect's id. |
| **~~Attack-roll-buff condition~~** ✓ shipped | 3 wired (blur, mirror-image, pass-without-trace). Mirror Image's duplicate-pool wired in slice 124; slice 125 closed the trigger-dispatch follow-up; slice 127 wired the RAW vision-gate. | Blur and Pass Without Trace shipped as composite-buff conditions in slice 73 (no engine change). Mirror Image needed a dedicated attack-deflection-pool primitive: new `MirrorImageDeflectedEvent` + reducer, `findMirrorImage` derive helper, and an intercept in `planAttack` + `planOffHandAttack` that rolls the deflection d20 before the attack d20 and (on redirect-success) rolls the attack against duplicate AC = 10 + bearer DEX mod. Hits emit `AttackRolled { hit: false }` + `MirrorImageDeflected { duplicateHit }`, with a follow-up `ConditionRemoved` when the pool empties. Bearer-side retaliation riders (AoA, Fire Shield) don't double-fire because the AttackRolled is stamped hit=false. Slice 125 routes the deflected AttackRolled through `dispatchTriggers` so attacker-side on-miss / on-attack riders (Studied Attacks' consume-on-attack-vs-source, future similar) fire as RAW expects. New optional `appliedConditionLevel` on `SpellBuffMechanicSchema` lets a buff stamp an initial pool count at cast time (Mirror Image: 3). Slice 127 wired GrantSense into the accumulator and added the RAW bypass: attackers with `blindsight` or `truesight` (any range), or attackers carrying the Blinded condition, skip the deflection branch entirely. The cast-spell attack-mechanic path (rare in practice) remains a documented deferral. |
| **~~Recurring-save primitive~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 5 wired across two slices (slice 92: bestow-curse's inactive-turn variant via `onFail: 'consumeAction'`; slice 93: hold-person, hold-monster, tashas-hideous-laughter, confusion via `onSuccess: 'removeCondition'`). | Slice 92 added the `recurringSave` field on `ConditionSchema` (ability + trigger + onFail) plus `engine.plan.tickRecurringSave`, which the consumer fires at the trigger moment (start / end of the bearer's turn) for any condition that declares the metadata. The planner rolls a save against the source caster's spell DC (sourceCharacterId on the applied condition, set by spell planners since slice 88) and on failure consumes the bearer's action when in an active encounter. Slice 93 extended the schema with an optional `onSuccess: 'removeCondition'` variant; the planner emits `ConditionRemoved` on a successful tick, modeling the "spell ends on the target" branch shared by Hold Person, Hold Monster, Hideous Laughter, and Confusion. `onFail` was relaxed to optional in the same slice — the Zod schema now requires at least one of `onFail` / `onSuccess`. Hideous Laughter's damage-taken extra-save-with-advantage branch and Hold Person's higher-level multi-target shape are still unwired; Confusion's random-action table also remains narrative-only. |
| **~~Type-conditional buff / ward~~** ✓ shipped | 3 wired full-RAW (protection-from-evil-and-good, magic-circle, holy-aura). Slice 103 shipped the disadvantage-on-attackers arm; slice 104 closed the source-gated condition-immunity arm. PfEoG's RAW "possessed by them" clause stays narrative (the engine doesn't carry a `possessed` condition). | Slice 103 extended `ImposeDisadvantageOnAttackers` to honor its existing `condition?: Predicate` field: the EffectAccumulator stores per-entry predicates, and `imposesDisadvantageOnAttackers(attackerFacts)` filters them against caller-supplied facts. The attack planner passes `attackerCreatureType` (resolved via `getCreatureType(attacker, content)` — monster.type via statblockId for creatures, species.creatureType for PCs / NPCs, default Humanoid). Slice 103 also added an `event.attackerCreatureType` fact in `dispatchTriggers.buildEventFacts` and a new `ApplyConditionToAttacker` TriggerAction variant that retargets the emitted ConditionApplied to the attacker. Slice 104 added a `condition?: Predicate` field to `GrantConditionImmunity` plus a `sourceCharacterId` parameter on `isImmuneToCondition`: the helper builds a `sourceCreatureType` fact from the source's record and threads it into `hasConditionImmunity(id, sourceFacts)`. All three call sites pass `sourceCharacterId` (cast-spell save + buff branches with `intent.characterId`; concentration aura tick with `intent.casterId`). Holy Aura uses both arms — universal ImposeDisadvantageOnAttackers + universal save-advantage on the condition's effects, plus an OnEvent rider with an `event.attackerCreatureType in ['Fiend', 'Undead']` filter emitting `ApplyConditionToAttacker { blinded }`. PfEoG and Magic Circle share an `any`-of-six-types predicate on both the attack-disadvantage and the charmed/frightened-immunity arms (`attackerCreatureType` and `sourceCreatureType` respectively). Magic Circle's RAW caster-choice-of-type isn't modeled (broader than RAW: the ward applies against all six types regardless of caster intent). |
| **~~AddDamageToAttacker TriggerAction~~** ✓ shipped | 2 wired: fire-shield (warm/chill) plus armor-of-agathys (slice 122, gated on `bearer.tempHp` > 0 via the new `gt` predicate). Both retaliate on melee attacks only (slice 123). | Slice 100 adds the `AddDamageToAttacker` TriggerAction variant of the existing AddDamage shape (same dice + damageType fields); the dispatcher's new `fireAddDamageToAttacker` helper builds a DamageApplied targeting `event.attackerId` instead of `event.targetId`. Crits on the triggering attack don't double the retaliation dice per RAW. Only fires against AttackRolled triggers. Slice 122 extends the dispatcher with a `bearer.tempHp` fact + the predicate-DSL `gt` / `gte` kinds so "while temp HP > 0" retaliation gates work — RAW-approximate since the engine doesn't track temp-HP provenance. Slice 123 adds a required `attackKind: 'melee' \| 'ranged'` field on `AttackRolledEvent` (populated from the weapon definition) + the `event.attackKind` fact, and AoA + Fire Shield (warm / chill) all add a fourth `eq event.attackKind melee` clause on their retaliation filters. Ranged attackers no longer trigger retaliation; thrown weapons still classify as melee since the engine doesn't track thrown-vs-melee-strike intent. |
| **~~Heal-blocking primitive~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 1 wired (spirit-shroud's "target can't regain HP until start of caster's next turn" rider on its three variants). Future content (e.g. spells / monster abilities that ward against healing) plugs in by adding a condition with `BlockHealing`. | Slice 98 adds a `BlockHealing` Effect kind (marker — no parameters), an `EffectAccumulator.hasHealingBlocked()` query, and an `isHealingBlocked(state, content, targetId)` derive helper. `planHealMechanic` consults the helper before emitting Healed; when blocked, the planner emits Healed with `amount: 0` (the existing `amount <= 0` reducer early-return makes it a no-op) plus a `(blocked)` annotation in the event's `source` field so the audit trail captures both intent and outcome. The slice also wires `ApplyCondition` TriggerAction dispatch in `fireTrigger` — previously only `AddDamage` was handled, so `ApplyCondition` actions on OnEvent riders silently dropped. Spirit Shroud's three variants gain a second TriggerAction (`{ kind: 'ApplyCondition', conditionId: 'healing-blocked-active', durationRounds: 1 }`) on each hit-rider. Slice 102 closed the auto-expiry loop: `fireApplyCondition` stamps `expiresOnRound = currentRound + durationRounds` on the emitted ConditionApplied (when inside an active encounter), and `planAdvanceTurn` sweeps every character's appliedConditions on each turn-start, emitting a `ConditionRemoved` for any whose `sourceCharacterId` matches the new active combatant and whose `expiresOnRound` is now in the past. Outside an encounter the expiry stays consumer-managed (currentRound is undefined). Other heal pathways (planTickRecurring's `effect: 'heal'` variant for Aura of Vitality; planAbsorbElements's compensating Healed) don't consult the gate yet; if those spells ever interact with blocked targets, a small follow-up gates them with the same helper. |
| **~~Cursed condition~~** ✓ shipped (slice 134) | 1 wired (remove-curse via the dedicated `planRemoveCurse` planner). | Slice 134 adds an optional `category: 'curse' \| 'disease' \| 'poison'` field on ConditionSchema (a small fixed enum matching the 2024 PHB's named removal interactions; future Lesser Restoration / Greater Restoration wire to 'disease' / 'poison' similarly). Bestow Curse's four `cursed-*-active` variants are tagged `category: 'curse'`; `planRemoveCurse` consumes a 3rd-level slot + an action, walks the touched target's appliedConditions, and emits a `ConditionRemoved` per match. No save, no roll, no spellcast attack roll (RAW: "any curse affecting that creature ends"). Bestow Curse's nested-ability-sub-choice variant (Cursed: Ability Score Disadvantage) is still narrative-only since the consumer carries the chosen ability out-of-band, but Remove Curse strips the condition either way. |
| **~~Directional attack advantage / disadvantage~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 1 wired (bestow-curse's attack-disadvantage variant via `cursed-attacks-active`). Lays groundwork for Sanctuary's pre-attack target-selection rider (still deferred — Sanctuary's WIS save fires before target selection, a different shape). | Slice 96 adds the `SetAdvantageVsSource` Effect kind (same `on` / `mode` shape as `SetAdvantage`, but only applies when the roll's counterparty equals the bearing applied condition's `sourceCharacterId`). BuilderContext gains an optional `sourceCharacterId` populated from the bearing AppliedCondition. EffectAccumulator gains `setAdvantageVsSource` / `advantageVsSource` (per-source advantage maps keyed on `${rollKey}::${sourceCharacterId}`). The attack planner consults `attackerEffects.advantageVsSource('attack', input.targetId)` and folds the result into the existing advantage / disadvantage resolution. Conditions without a stamped source drop the effect silently. |
| **~~Attacker-side `advantageFor('attack')` wiring~~** ✓ shipped | 6 conditions retro-wired (blinded, frightened, poisoned, prone, restrained — all gain disadvantage on their own attacks; invisible — gains advantage on its own attacks). Future content that emits a `SetAdvantage on:'attack'` plugs in without further engine work. | Slice 97 closes a latent bug: the existing six conditions already carried `SetAdvantage on:'attack'` effects, but the attack planner never consulted `attackerEffects.advantageFor('attack')`. The slice folds `advantageFor('attack').advantage` and `.disadvantage` into the planner's existing 2024-RAW advantage-cancellation resolution alongside the slice-96 per-source contributions. Pure engine wiring; no content changes. |
| **~~Resistance-buff condition~~** ✓ shipped | 1 wired (protection-from-energy). Future smites (e.g. Blade Ward, fire-shield's resistance arm) plug in by adding a condition with the matching `GrantResistance` effect. | Slice 95 confirmed the resistance-buff was a pure-content gap: `GrantResistance` already accepted a specific `DamageType`, `EffectAccumulator.addResistance` already routed it, and `mitigateDamage` already consulted `hasResistance` per type. Protection from Energy ships as five spell-bound `protection-X-active` conditions plus a `casterChoosesVariant` buff mechanic that picks one at cast time — same shape as Spirit Shroud (slice 89). |
| **~~Trap mechanic~~** ✓ shipped (partial) | 2 wired (glyph-of-warding Explosive Runes variant, cordon-of-arrows). Glyph of Warding's Spell Glyph variant (store an arbitrary spell whose targets are resolved at trigger time) still ships schema-only. | Slice 94 adds `TrapSchema` (id, label, sourceCharacterId, sourceSpellId, payload, chargesRemaining) plus a `traps: Record<TrapId, Trap>` collection on `CampaignState`. Three events: `TrapArmed` (stamps into state.traps), `TrapTriggered` (decrements charges), `TrapExpired` (removes from state). A new `trap` SpellMechanic prime-arms the trap at cast time; it carries the save ability + damage dice + halfOnSuccess + charges + label, and either a fixed `damageType` (Cordon: piercing), a `casterChoosesDamageType` allowed list (Glyph: acid / cold / fire / lightning / thunder), and either a `fixedDC` (Cordon: 13) or the caster's spell save DC at arm time (Glyph). The DC and damage type are pre-baked into the TrapArmed event so the trap is self-contained at trigger time (Glyph's 1-hour cast / until-dispelled lifecycle means the caster's stats may change between arming and triggering). A new `engine.plan.triggerTrap({trapId, triggeringCharacterId})` planner rolls the save, deals damage (halved on success when halfOnSuccess, zero on success when not), and emits TrapTriggered + (when charges hit zero) TrapExpired. |
| **~~Dedicated planner: Thunder Step~~** ✓ shipped | 1 wired (thunder-step). | Slice 128 adds `engine.plan.thunderStep` with the Misty Step skeleton (action economy + slot consume + teleport + occupancy / range / known-spell validation) plus the AoE payload: filter combatants within 10 ft of the caster's origin (excluding caster and ally), roll one 3d10 thunder pool (`+1d10` per slot above 3rd), emit per-target SaveRolled (CON vs caster spell DC) + DamageApplied (full / half on save). Optional ally argument enforces the RAW "willing creature within 5 ft" proximity gate and emits a second CombatantMoved at the tail. Spell-coverage skip retagged to "has dedicated planner." |
| **~~Resurrection / death utility~~** ✓ shipped | All 5 spells route through `engine.plan.resurrect` (revivify, raise-dead, reincarnate, resurrection, true-resurrection) | The resurrection primitive (`CharacterResurrected` event, `applyCharacterResurrected` reducer, `planResurrect` planner) was already in the engine — slice 80 just retagged the SPELL_EXPECTATIONS so the spell-coverage test stops claiming they're deferred. The planner validates target is at 0 HP, requires the right minimum slot level per spell (3 / 5 / 5 / 7 / 9), consumes the slot, and emits CharacterResurrected with `hpAfter` (default 1) and optional `newSpeciesId` (for Reincarnate). Time-since-death gates (Revivify: 1 min; Raise Dead: 10 days; True Resurrection: 200 years) are consumer-side narrative state. |
| **~~Scrying / divination utility~~** ✓ shipped (slices 135 + 136) | 2 wired (clairvoyance via `planClairvoyance`, scrying via `planScrying`). | Slice 135 adds a `Sensor` runtime entity (`state.sensors: Record<SensorId, Sensor>`) modeled on the slice-94 Trap shape: id + label + free-text location + casterId + sourceSpellId + sourceEffectInstanceId + sight/hearing mode. Three new events (`RemoteSensorPlaced`, `RemoteSensorModeChanged`, `RemoteSensorRemoved`) drive the lifecycle; reducers in `src/engine/reducers/sensor.ts`. `planClairvoyance` emits the action + slot + concentration + sensor place sequence; `planSwitchSensorMode` toggles seeing / hearing on the caster's action; `planRemoveSensor` ends the spell voluntarily. `clearConcentrationEffect` sweeps sensors linked to a dropped concentration via `sourceEffectInstanceId`, mirroring the item-buff sweep added in slice 76. Slice 136 added `planScrying`: composes the sensor primitive with a target WIS save against the caster's spell DC (with optional `dcAdjustment` from RAW's familiarity tier table); on fail the sensor is placed with `location: "near <target name>"` and concentration starts, on success the spell fizzles and the slot is still consumed. The save passes `sourceIsMagical: true` so Magic Resistance is honored. The engine doesn't model perception, "sensor follows target" position, or the RAW 24-hour cooldown after a successful save (all consumer territory). |
| **~~Illusion-interaction primitive~~** ✓ shipped (slice 137) | 2 wired (silent-image, major-image). | Slice 137 adds an `Illusion` runtime entity (`state.illusions: Record<IllusionId, Illusion>`) modeled on the slice-94 Trap / slice-135 Sensor pattern: id + label + free-text location + `kind: 'visual' \| 'audiovisual'` + casterId + sourceSpellId + sourceEffectInstanceId + baked `investigationDC` (caster's spell save DC at cast time) + `disbelievedBy: CharacterId[]`. Three new events (`IllusionCreated`, `IllusionInvestigated`, `IllusionDismissed`) drive the lifecycle. Four planners: `planSilentImage` (1st-level visual), `planMajorImage` (3rd-level audiovisual), `planInvestigateIllusion` (action + INT (Investigation) check vs the baked DC, on success adds the investigator to `disbelievedBy`), `planDismissIllusion` (voluntary spell end). `clearConcentrationEffect` sweeps illusions linked to a dropped concentration via `sourceEffectInstanceId`. The engine surfaces the disbelief set; consumers / DMs decide what disbelieving creatures see and act on. RAW edge cases not modeled this slice: caster's bonus-action move (Silent Image) / action-rechange (Major Image) of the illusion's shape (consumer-side or a future schema extension); the 6th-level-slot permanent-no-concentration upgrade for Major Image. |
| **~~Push / aerial-restraint primitives~~** ✓ shipped | 2 wired (gust-of-wind, earthbind) | Slice 78 adds a `CreaturePushed` event (informational, like TriggerFired — the engine doesn't model positions, so the consumer applies the position change). The save mechanic gains an optional `pushedFeetOnFail` field that emits the event per failed target. Gust of Wind wires as STR save + 15 ft push. Earthbind wires the aerial restraint via a save → `earthbound-active` condition with `ModifySpeed mode:'fly' op:'set' value:0`; slice 77's getEffectiveSpeed retrofit ensures the fly-zero actually applies. The "falls when grounded" portion of Earthbind is consumer-side (falling damage). |

Picking from this list, top three by spell-count payoff: summon system (11+), area-effect mechanic (~13), on-hit trigger (~9). The other primitives each unblock smaller cohorts; bundle them together by primitive when their turn comes.

## How this list is maintained

At the close of each content slice, update the relevant section here and bump the "Coverage at a glance" counts. If the slice introduces a new mechanic kind (e.g. a future reaction-spell primitive), retro-update the affected schema-only spells to either `wired` or move them to a different deferred bucket. When an engine slice from the "Future engine slices" table ships, mark it as done and walk the affected spells in this doc to their new status.
